Bracket UI is a UI-heavy piece that benefits from real season data and from observing how commissioners use the new generator; standings-with-phase-filter is already in place, so playoff games can be inserted manually today and they'll be cleanly excluded from regular-season standings.

**One migration** (live in prod via MCP):

**`league_games_add_phase_for_playoffs`** тАФ adds `league_games.phase text NOT NULL DEFAULT 'regular_season' CHECK (phase IN ('regular_season','playoffs'))`. All 42 pre-existing rows backfilled to `regular_season` via the column default. New composite index `league_games_league_phase_idx ON (league_id, phase)` for the standings view's hot read path. The `league_standings` view (already flipped to `security_invoker=on` per May 18 fix) was dropped + recreated with `WHERE league_games.phase = 'regular_season'` in both branches of the UNION ALL тАФ playoff games are now structurally invisible to regular-season standings. `security_invoker=on` preserved.

**Advisor pass:** 62 WARN, **0 ERROR-level**, no new warnings introduced. View def re-pulled with `pg_get_viewdef` confirms the `phase = 'regular_season'` predicate is in place.

**Code (1 new lib, 3 modified):**

- **New** `src/lib/leagueScheduleGenerator.js` тАФ pure-function schedule generator. Three exports:
  - `computeScheduleShape({ teamCount, targetGamesPerTeam })` тЖТ `{ meetingsPerPair, gamesPerTeam, totalGames }`. Rounds the user's target to the nearest clean round-robin count (so "30 games per team across 8 teams" = `round(30/7)=4` meetings = 28 games per team). Floors at 1 meeting so a low target always produces at least one full RR.
  - `buildSlotTimeline({ startDate, daysOfWeek, gamesPerDay, totalSlots, firstPuckHour, firstPuckMinute, gameBlockMinutes })` тЖТ array of ISO datetime strings. Walks the calendar forward from `startDate`, emits up to `gamesPerDay` slots on each allowed day-of-week, stagger by `gameBlockMinutes`. Hard-capped at 3 years of walk so a misconfigured form can't spin forever; returns `error: 'calendar_exhausted'` signal.
  - `generateLeagueSchedule({ teams, targetGamesPerTeam, startDate, daysOfWeek, gamesPerDay, rinkId, ... })` тЖТ `{ rows, shape, lastSlotDate, error? }`. Reuses `roundRobinPairs` from `tournamentManage.js` for the underlying RR. Flips home/away on alternating meetings so a team that hosts a given opponent in meeting 1 visits them in meeting 2 тАФ fairness across multiple round-robins. Tags every row with `phase: 'regular_season'`. Caller does the DB insert.
- `src/lib/scheduleBuilder.js` тАФ extended `bulkInsertLeagueGames` to write `phase: g.phase || 'regular_season'` so the new generator's rows land tagged correctly. Default matches the DB column default; the (future) bracket generator can pass `'playoffs'`.
- `src/pages/LeagueManage.js` тАФ Schedule tab now leads with **тЪб Smart Generator тАФ Target Games Per Team**. Inline `SmartScheduleGenerator` sub-component with:
  - Target games per team (number, 1-200)
  - Start date
  - Days-of-week multi-select chips (Sun-Sat)
  - Games per day (default 1)
  - Rink picker (optional тАФ generator allows commissioner to assign per-game later)
  - First puck (24h hour + minute) + minutes between games (default 18:00 + 75-min spacing)
  - **Live preview card** that re-runs `generateLeagueSchedule` on every form change (no DB hit) тАФ shows "X games across Y teams. Each team plays each opponent N├Ч = M games per team. Last game: <date>." Surfaces `calendar_exhausted` error if days-of-week + start can't fit the schedule in 3 years.
  - Two-tap confirm тАФ first tap shows "Confirm тАФ insert N games", second tap actually inserts via `bulkInsertLeagueGames`. Prevents accidental double-generation.
  - The existing modal-based "Advanced тАФ Single/Double Round-Robin Wizard" stays accessible just below as the secondary path for commissioners who want finer control. Both write through `bulkInsertLeagueGames`, so both produce `phase='regular_season'`-tagged rows.
- `src/pages/LeagueCreate.js` тАФ `FORMAT_PRESETS` expanded from 1 to **4 presets**:
  - `classic_league` (unchanged) тАФ single RR, 3├Ч12 stop, 6-goal mercy, ties allowed
  - `beer_league_no_ties` тАФ 3├Ч17 run-time, SO in regular season, no mercy
  - `high_school_style` тАФ 3├Ч15 stop, 7-goal mercy, OT/SO playoffs only
  - `youth_short_game` тАФ 2├Ч20 run-time, 8-goal mercy, ties allowed, no SO

**Build:** clean. Bundle +2.37 kB gz on top of Phase 2.

### May 19, 2026 evening (continued, fourth pass) тАФ League engine Phase 3b: playoff bracket UI

Closes the last queued piece of Phase 3 from the original build doc. Layered on the same `claude/laughing-nightingale-10d576` worktree тАФ Phase 1 + 2 + 3a + 3b ship as one merge.

**One migration** (live in prod via MCP):

**`league_games_add_round_for_playoff_bracket`** тАФ adds `league_games.round text NULL` (mirror of `games.round` on the tournament side; intentionally no CHECK so non-standard bracket patterns like play-ins or third-place games can land later without a schema change). Adds partial composite index `league_games_phase_round_idx ON (league_id, phase, round) WHERE phase='playoffs'` so "list this league's playoff bracket" stays cheap as regular-season rows pile up around it.

**Structural constraint discovered:** `league_games.home_team_id` + `away_team_id` are **NOT NULL** (vs tournament `games` which allows NULL). Means I can't pre-create TBD placeholder rounds the way the tournament bracket does. Phase 3b ships a **one-round-at-a-time** flow: commissioner generates round 1 from standings (real seeds), then comes back after that round finalizes to generate round 2 from winners. This is actually a cleaner UX than placeholder-fill тАФ commissioners can adjust schedule between rounds based on real availability.

**Advisor pass:** 62 WARN, **0 ERROR-level**, no new findings. All 42 existing rows untouched (still tagged `regular_season`).

**Code (1 new lib, 1 modified):**

- **New** `src/lib/leaguePlayoffGenerator.js` тАФ pure-function bracket generator.
  - `SUPPORTED_BRACKET_SIZES = [2, 4, 8]` тАФ covers the vast majority of beer/youth/adult-rec leagues; 16+ is a Phase 4 ask if needed.
  - `seedPairs(bracketSize)` тАФ standard 1v8 / 4v5 / 3v6 / 2v7 (8-team QFs); 1v4 / 2v3 (4-team semis); 1v2 (2-team final). Higher seed = home team.
  - `firstRoundLabel(bracketSize)` тАФ `'quarterfinal' | 'semifinal' | 'final' | null`.
  - `generatePlayoffRoundOne({ standings, bracketSize, ...scheduling })` тАФ seeds from current `league_standings` rows (sorted by `rank`). Reuses `buildSlotTimeline` from `leagueScheduleGenerator.js` for the calendar walk. Returns `{ rows, label, error? }` with `error тИИ { 'unsupported_bracket_size', 'not_enough_teams', 'calendar_exhausted' }`.
  - `generatePlayoffNextRound({ previousRound, bracketSize, includeBronze, ...scheduling })` тАФ takes finalized round-N games + emits round-N+1 by pairing adjacent-slot winners (`[w0,w1]` тЖТ final, `[w0,w1,w2,w3]` тЖТ 2 semis). When previousRound is `'semifinal'` and `includeBronze=true`, also emits a bronze game pairing the two losers. Validates: previous round must all be `status='final'`, no ties (return `'incomplete_winners'`), no slot exhaustion.
  - All rows tagged `phase='playoffs'` + the correct round label so the standings view structurally excludes them (Phase 3a).
- `src/pages/LeagueManage.js`:
  - New 'Playoffs' tab in `MANAGE_TABS = ['Teams', 'Schedule', 'Playoffs', 'Settings']`.
  - `load()` extended to fetch `getLeagueStandings(id)` alongside teams/games/rinks. New `standings` state.
  - New `<PlayoffsTab>` inline sub-component (~270 lines) with three sections:
    - **ЁЯПЖ Generate Playoff Bracket** form тАФ bracket size selector (2/4/8, disabled options for sizes that exceed team count), days-of-week chips, start date, games-per-day, rink, first puck, spacing. Live preview shows actual matchups with team names + dates. Two buttons render conditionally:
      - **Round 1** ("Generate quarterfinal/semifinal/final (N games)") when no round-1 games exist yet тАФ seeded from standings.
      - **Next round** ("Generate semifinal/final (N games)") when the latest existing round is fully final тАФ pairs winners + optional bronze-game checkbox for semis-complete state.
    - **Top N from Standings (Seeding)** тАФ read-only preview showing which teams currently hold the top seeds and their W-L-T-pts. Surfaces "Only X teams have a standings rank тАФ need N for this bracket size" when standings is short.
    - **Current Bracket** тАФ grouped by round (Quarterfinals тЖТ Semifinals тЖТ Final / Bronze) with home/away/time/score (when final). Renders only when at least one playoff game exists.
  - The `<SmartScheduleGenerator>` (Phase 3a) and existing modal-based Advanced wizard stay in the Schedule tab тАФ Playoffs is a separate flow.

**Build:** clean. Bundle +3.5 kB gz on top of Phase 3a.

**DB smoke (all pass):**
- тЬЕ `round` column added (nullable text), partial index `league_games_phase_round_idx` built.
- тЬЕ View definition still contains `phase = 'regular_season'` filter.
- тЬЕ All 42 existing rows untouched; `round` defaults to NULL for them.
- тЬЕ Advisor pass: 0 ERROR-level.
- тЬЕ Generator math verified by inspection: seedPairs for 2/4/8 returns standard cross-bracket matchups; `pairWinnersInOrder([w0,w1,w2,w3])` тЖТ `[(w0,w1), (w2,w3)]`; tie detection blocks next-round generation cleanly.

**Smoke-tests deferred to Pete (browser):**
1. Open `/league/<id>/manage` тЖТ Playoffs tab; with at least 4 finalized regular-season games, expect 4-team bracket option active; pick start date + Sun chip; preview shows "1v4" + "2v3" matchups with correct seeds; tap Generate; expect 2 rows inserted with `phase='playoffs'` + `round='semifinal'`.
2. Finalize both semifinal games in ScorerView; come back to Playoffs tab; expect the "Next round preview" panel to show the championship matchup (winner of semi 1 vs winner of semi 2) + bronze checkbox; tap Generate; expect 2 rows (final + bronze) tagged correctly.

### May 19, 2026 evening (continued, fifth pass) тАФ Activation gate (monetization switch)

Pete realized that everything functions for everyone тАФ there's no paywall in the loop. Closes that with a **per-event activation switch** that gates the live-scoring + push value paths at the RLS layer. Organizers can still create + configure freely (teams, schedule, bracket, public landing); only the things that matter at game-time (finalize, goal/penalty inserts, push fanout) require a Rinkd admin to flip `is_activated` first. Layered on the same `claude/laughing-nightingale-10d576` worktree.

**One migration** (live in prod via MCP):

**`tournaments_and_leagues_add_is_activated_admin_gate`** тАФ adds `is_activated boolean NOT NULL DEFAULT false` to both `public.tournaments` and `public.leagues`. **Backfilled all existing rows to `true`** (4 tournaments + 5 leagues) so BLPA Cleveland / CSHL personal tracker / demo data keep working. New rows default `false` тАФ Pete decides per event going forward.

Three RLS rewrites enforce the gate:
- `games_director_update` + `games_scorer_update` (tournament side): both now require `EXISTS tournaments t WHERE t.id = games.tournament_id AND t.is_activated = true` ANDed onto the existing director/scorer path. The `tournament_id IS NULL` escape hatch (solo / non-tournament games) stays exempt.
- `league_games_update`: same gate ANDed onto the existing commissioner/scorekeeper/scorer path.
- New `game_goals_insert_requires_activated` + `game_penalties_insert_requires_activated`: defense-in-depth INSERT policies. A goal/penalty insert hits a game; that game's parent tournament OR league must be activated (or the game must be solo `tournament_id IS NULL`). Blocks the scoring-tool write path even if UPDATE somehow bypasses.

**DB smoke test** confirmed the gate works end-to-end: set BLPA Cleveland `is_activated=false`, attempted `UPDATE games SET home_score=99 WHERE tournament_id=...` as the founding director тАФ **0 rows affected**. Flipped `is_activated=true` and retried тАФ **12 rows updated** (one per pool game). Cleaned up.

**Advisor pass:** 62 WARN, **0 ERROR-level**, no new findings from this migration.

**Code (1 new page, 1 new route, edits across 5 files, 2 Edge Function redeploys):**

- **New** `src/pages/AdminActivations.js` (~220 lines) тАФ admin console at `/admin/activations`. Gated by `useIsRinkdAdmin` (same `profiles.is_admin=true` gate the other admin pages use). Lists tournaments + leagues with:
  - Logo + name + division/season/date subtitle.
  - Status pill (тЧП Activated green / тЧЛ Pending amber).
  - Toggle switch.
  - Filter chips (Pending / Activated / All) + free-text search across name + division.
  - "Pending (N)" counter on the Pending chip.
  - Click name тЖТ deep-link to the public page.
  - Reload button + error surface for write failures.
- `src/App.js` тАФ registered `/admin/activations` route + `AdminActivations` import.
- `src/components/MoreDrawer.js` тАФ added Activations link to the Rinkd Admin section between Analytics and Bug reports.
- `src/pages/Tournament.js` тАФ "ЁЯФТ Activation pending" pill next to "тЧП Live now" in the page header when `tournament.is_activated === false`.
- `src/pages/League.js` тАФ same pill next to the IN SEASON status pill.
- `src/pages/TournamentManage.js` тАФ yellow callout banner under the page header explaining the activation requirement and linking to `hello@rinkd.app`.
- `src/pages/LeagueManage.js` тАФ same callout banner. Both managers explicitly call out that **setup still works** тАФ only live scoring + pushes are locked.
- `src/pages/ScorerView.js`:
  - Load query selects `is_activated` on the joined tournament/league.
  - New gate page renders after the "Scorer access only" gate: if parent not activated, shows "ЁЯФТ Activation pending тАФ Email hello@rinkd.app" with a back button. Doesn't render the scorer UI so users don't stare at a console that silently refuses every write.
- `send-recap-push` Edge Function (v2, ACTIVE, JWT enforced) тАФ added `is_activated` to the tournament join + returns `{ sent: 0, reason: 'tournament_not_activated' }` early if false. No push fanout for non-activated events.
- `send-league-recap-push` Edge Function (v2, ACTIVE, JWT enforced) тАФ same gate via league lookup. Returns `{ sent: 0, reason: 'league_not_activated' }`.

**Build:** clean (+2.7 kB gz on top of Phase 3b).

**How it works end-to-end:**
1. Organizer signs up + creates a tournament/league via the existing wizards. `is_activated=false` by default.
2. They can add teams, generate schedule, build bracket, customize everything. Public landing page shows their event. The "Activation pending" pill is visible everywhere.
3. They contact `hello@rinkd.app` (the banner copy points them here) and pay.
4. Pete opens `/admin/activations`, finds the event in the Pending list, taps the toggle. `is_activated тЖТ true`.
5. Live scoring + auto-recap pushes unlock immediately. Director/scorers can finalize games. Recap posts fan out to push subscribers.
6. If a refund/dispute lands, Pete flips the toggle back to false. Scoring re-locks. No data loss.

**Smoke-tests deferred to Pete (browser):**
1. Open `/admin/activations` тАФ expect all 4 tournaments + 5 leagues showing тЧП Activated (backfill).
2. Toggle BLPA Cleveland off; load the tournament page in another tab тАФ expect "ЁЯФТ Activation pending" pill. Open TournamentManage тАФ yellow callout banner. Open ScorerView for any game тАФ expect the activation-pending wall (not the scorer console). Toggle back on; reload; everything restored.
3. Create a fresh test league via `/league/create` тАФ expect `is_activated=false` default. Try to score тЖТ wall. Activate тЖТ unlocks.
4. As a non-admin user, navigate to `/admin/activations` тАФ expect the "ЁЯФТ Activations is Rinkd staff only" gate.

**Defense-in-depth layers (in order):**
- **RLS** (the security): can't UPDATE games / INSERT goals / INSERT penalties without parent activated. Server enforces.
- **Edge Functions** (defense in depth): both push functions refuse to fan out for non-activated events.
- **UX banners** (the usability): pills, callouts, ScorerView wall so users understand why writes fail.

**тЬЕ MERGED to main May 19 evening** as part of `5eedabd0`. Activation panel + RLS gate live in prod.

### May 20, 2026 тАФ League-customer day: KOHA onboarding + roster/manager flows + fixes

A full day shipping straight to `main` (post-merge) driven by standing up **KOHA (Kanata Oldtimers Hockey Association)** тАФ the first real external league. Each item below is its own commit; all live in prod.

**Turnstile login fix (`af13dfab` + `ebd4f7ca`) тАФ was breaking ALL logins.** The May 18 Turnstile rollout enabled CAPTCHA Protection globally at the Supabase project level but only rendered the widget on signup step 3. Every `/auth/v1/signin` + `/recover` was returning `captcha protection: request disallowed (no captcha_token found)`. Fix: render `<TurnstileWidget>` on the login + forgot-password forms; `signIn` + `resetPasswordForEmail` forward the token; widget remounts via a `turnstileResetKey` after a failed attempt (consumed tokens) + on mode switch. Found via the analytics funnel тАФ 13 "login failures" were one session pounding the broken wall.

**AdminActivations fixes (`dbf64d33`, `73bf3c52`).** (a) The page SELECTed `logo_color`/`logo_initials` from tournaments, which don't exist there (only leagues have them; tournaments use `accent_color`). Split the SELECTs + normalized avatar fields at render. (b) Toggling an event you didn't found silently no-op'd тАФ the `tournaments`/`leagues` UPDATE RLS gates on founder, not Rinkd-admin. Added `admin_set_activation(p_kind, p_id, p_value)` SECURITY DEFINER RPC gated on `profiles.is_admin`; the panel calls it instead of a direct UPDATE.

**Hosting banners gated (`42344635`).** "Run your league on Rinkd" / "Host your tournament on Rinkd" CTAs in the Info tabs now hide when `is_activated === true` тАФ they're lead-gen, wrong to show a paying customer.

**Funnel instrumentation (`06e2ed8a`).** Added `auth_view`, `auth_first_input`, `signup_step_advanced`, `forgot_password_clicked`, `tournament_public_view`, `league_public_view`. The middle of the landingтЖТsignup funnel was a black box; these close it. Note: a large share of top-of-funnel may come via shared tournament/league URLs (which fire `*_public_view`, NOT `landing_view`), so compare those when reading the funnel.

**Per-game stream URL (`a69702f1`, migration `league_games_and_rinks_add_youtube_url`).** KOHA streams on YouTube, not LiveBarn. Added `youtube_url` to `league_games` + `rinks` (rink = default, game = override). New `src/lib/streamUrl.js` detects platform (YouTube/Twitch/Facebook/Vimeo/other) тЖТ labels the "тЦ╢ Watch on X" button + brand color. Independent of LiveBarn тАФ a game can show both buttons. Generic despite the column name; only league side (mirrors `live_barn_venue_id` which also skips tournament `games`).

**League logo upload (`f2f5252c`).** The LeagueCreate wizard had upload from Phase 1, but the Settings tab on existing leagues didn't. Added the same 5MB + NSFW + uploadMedia flow to LeagueManage Settings. Wired `logo_url` rendering through League.js banner + Leagues.js index (PublicLeagueLanding + AdminActivations already rendered it).

**DatePicker timezone fix (`5eca7c4e`).** `new Date("2026-06-13")` parses as UTC midnight тЖТ renders the day before in Eastern. `parseLocalDate` now constructs via `new Date(y, m-1, d)` for date-only strings. Global fix тАФ TournamentCreate + LeagueCreate both use the shared component.

**League-added teams are now real teams (`3db0aa7f`, migration `create_league_team_rpc_and_koha_backfill`).** Previously `LeagueManage` added unlinked `league_teams` rows (`team_id` NULL) тАФ invisible on `/teams`, can't have a manager/roster. New `create_league_team(league_id, name, color, initials, division)` SECURITY DEFINER RPC (gated on `is_league_commissioner`) creates a real `public.teams` row (manager_id NULL = unclaimed, is_public true) + the link. `handleAddUnlinkedTeam` calls it. **KOHA's 8 teams backfilled** in the migration. (cshl + test-team-3e demos left unlinked.)

**Commissioner-grants-management UI (`a5936dce`, migration `assign_league_team_manager_rpc`).** LeagueManage Teams tab: each row shows manager status (Unclaimed / тЬУ Manager: @handle) + a "+ Manager" / "+ Co-manager" inline form. `assign_league_team_manager(league_id, team_id, user_id)` RPC (SECURITY DEFINER, gated on commissioner + team-in-league) inserts `team_members(role=manager)` + promotes to founder if `manager_id` is NULL; else adds as co-manager (multi-team-manager pattern). `getLeagueTeams` now embeds `manager:profiles!teams_manager_id_fkey`. New lib `src/lib/leagueTeamManagers.js`.

**Email-invite path for team-manager grants (`90f6666d`, migration `team_manager_invites_email_path`).** When the target has no Rinkd account: `create_team_manager_invite` RPC mints a single-use 14-day token; `send-invite` Edge Function (v10, new `team_manager_invite` type) emails a magic link to `/accept-team-invite?token=тАж`. New `AcceptTeamInvite.js` page: signed-out тЖТ bounce to `/login?returnTo` (token survives); signed-in тЖТ `accept_team_manager_invite(token)` validates token (exists/unconsumed/unexpired/**email matches**) + grants. Both RPCs SECURITY DEFINER.

**Join-request flow review + fixes (`434ad328`).** Found: unclaimed teams (KOHA) couldn't have join requests actioned тАФ no manager existed + commissioner had no RLS path. The live HowitzerтЖТCemented request was stuck. Added `is_league_commissioner_of_team(team_id, user_id)` helper; broadened `team_join_requests` read+update + `team_members` insert RLS to OR it in. Rewrote `notify_team_manager_on_join_request` to fan out to ALL managers + ALL league commissioners (was `LIMIT 1`), deduped, with locked search_path. `Team.js` now hydrates `joinRequested` from the DB on mount (was reload-resets-to-fresh-button).

**Team-roster loop closed (`01894320`, migration `notify_requester_on_join_decision`).** (a) New AFTER UPDATE trigger fires a notification to the REQUESTER on approve ("You've been added to X. Welcome to the roster.") or deny. Two new notification kinds registered in `KIND_META`. (b) `TeamManage.handleAddMember` now fires the `team_invite` email when a manager adds a player by email with no matching account тАФ the existing `link_invited_player` auth trigger auto-fills `user_id` + flips status active on signup, so the email just motivates the signup.

### May 20, 2026 тАФ Pricing model locked: per-season / per-event ladders. BIZ-TIER-1 SUPERSEDED.

Pete delivered a clean pricing guide (`docs/Rinkd_Pricing_Guide.docx`) that **replaces the May 17 BIZ-TIER-1 BenchBoss-arrangement model**. The new structure is simpler, easier to communicate, easier to bill, and aligns cleanly with the activation gate's binary toggle (one tier choice per activation event).

**Leagues тАФ per-season fee, all features unlocked:**
| Tier | Teams | $/season |
|---|---|---|
| Starter | тЙд6 | $299 |
| **Standard** тнР most popular | тЙд12 | $599 |
| Pro | тЙд20 | $999 |
| Division add-on | +1 division | +$99 |

**Tournaments тАФ per-event fee:**
| Tier | Teams | $/event |
|---|---|---|
| Small | тЙд8 | $149 |
| Standard | тЙд16 | $299 |
| Large | тЙд24 | $499 |
| Premier | 25+ | $799 |

**Cross-sell:**
- Year 1: first tournament FREE with any active league plan.
- Year 2+: 15% off all tournaments for active league members.

**Registration (when LA-1 / TOURN-REG-1 ship):**
- Platform fee: **1%** (down from the old 1.5-2% in BIZ-TIER-1).
- Payment processing: 2.9% + $0.30, **passed through at cost to the registrant at checkout** тАФ no organizer absorption, no Rinkd markup. (Reverses the May 17 decision where organizer absorbed Stripe fees.)

**What this changes vs the old model:**
1. **BIZ-TIER-1 is dead.** Old "Community / Organizer-pays / Pass-through / Pro" framework superseded тАФ see updated row in ┬з7.
2. **Registration math shifted** тАФ 1% platform fee, registrant absorbs Stripe.
3. **Activation gate maps cleanly to a tier** тАФ each `is_activated=true` flip is implicitly a "Pete picked a tier at billing time" event. Currently the admin UI is binary; tier enforcement (team caps, upgrade prompts) is a Sprint-2 follow-up тАФ defer until the first paying customer.
4. **BLPA Cleveland is explicitly OUT of this ladder.** Stays as a custom deal Pete is still negotiating; BIZ-BLPA-1 row updated to reflect "TBD custom contract".

**No code changes from this update** тАФ pure docs + pricing alignment. The activation gate already exists; tier-enforcement build comes later.

### May 20, 2026 (continued) тАФ Pre-pilot scale / reliability / security audit + fixes

Ran a full scale/cost/reliability pass (two code-audit agents over the data layer + Edge Functions, plus Supabase perf + security advisors and table-size checks). **Headline: the foundation is solid and nothing is breaking at scale** тАФ both advisors are 0-ERROR; the largest table is `analytics_events` at 500 rows; feed pagination + embedded selects are already in place; push fanout is parallel + per-recipient isolated; ScorerView's write path is clean; email crons are idempotent via ledger tables. Five commits shipped straight to main + 2 Edge Function deploys + 1 migration. HEAD `ff792c5d`.

**ЁЯФ┤ Security тАФ `submit-scoresheet` Edge Function hardened (`b52cb60c` + `ff792c5d`, deployed v8).** It ran on service-role but never verified the caller and took the recipient `manager_emails` straight from the request body тАФ so any authenticated user could make `hello@rinkd.app` email an arbitrary PDF attachment to arbitrary addresses (domain-reputation abuse) and overwrite `scoresheet_url` on any game (tampering). Now: caller identified from JWT (`getUser(token)`); authorized for the specific game via assigned `scorekeeper_id` OR `is_tournament_director` / `is_league_commissioner` OR an assigned role-scorer (`tournament_roles`/`league_roles`) тАФ a faithful mirror of the `games_update`/`league_games_update` RLS; recipients resolved server-side from the game's own teams (`tournament_teams.contact_email` / `league_teams`тЖТ`teams.manager_id`тЖТ`profiles.email`); body emails ignored. **тЪая╕П The happy path was NOT tested end-to-end** (couldn't mint a real director session JWT from Claude Code) тАФ see the new ┬з12 pre-pilot checklist item. Unauthorized path fails closed.

**ЁЯЯа Perf тАФ live-standings reload debounced (`dcb0afc6`).** `Tournament.js` + `League.js` re-ran the entire page load (incl. the standings view recompute) on every realtime `games`/`league_games` change тАФ so each goal tap by any scorer triggered a full reload for every spectator with the page open. Now coalesced into one reload per ~1.5s window. Same fix on both pages.

**ЁЯЯв Perf тАФ Profile page (`4e35d21d`).** Collapsed a ~6-call serial-await waterfall into one `Promise.all`; capped the previously-unbounded `posts SELECT *` at 50.

**ЁЯЯв Auth default (`9b50a41f`).** Cold landing traffic now opens the auth screen on signup instead of login (Landing passes `defaultMode="signup"`); `/login` still opens on login for returning-user intent (bookmarks, "sign in" links, `returnTo` invite flows). Motivated by the May 20 traffic review: all 12 auth-screen sessions that day opened in login mode and 7 bounced without typing.

**ЁЯЯв Observability (`b52cb60c`).** `send-recap-push` (v3) now logs non-410/404 push delivery failures with context (were silently swallowed); `submit-scoresheet` surfaces Resend email failures instead of reporting `success`.

**ЁЯЯв Security hygiene тАФ migration `lock_search_path_on_legacy_functions`.** Locked `search_path` on the 20 functions the advisor flagged `function_search_path_mutable` (incl. trigger functions like `bump_post_like_count`, `link_invited_player`, `notify_*`) тАФ closes the search-path-hijack class the ┬з9 trigger lesson warns about. 20/20 verified locked. All `public` except `mark_all_notifications_read` (`public, auth`).

**Deferred (not pilot-blocking, by decision):** `send-game-reminders` sequential email loop (only bites at ~100+ emails/hour); retry logic on web-push/email (crons self-heal); 100 `multiple_permissive_policies` advisor WARNs (behavior-affecting cleanup тАФ do deliberately, read each cluster); 4 unindexed FKs on `team_manager_invites` (trivial); leaked-password protection toggle (HaveIBeenPwned тАФ paid tier, Pete deferring until volume). The 33 `unused_index` INFO are expected at this data size тАФ don't drop them, they're forward-looking.

### May 21, 2026 тАФ GS-7 shipped (iOS PWA install banner); GS-3 held

**GS-7 тАФ iOS PWA install banner (`1efb2124`).** iOS Safari only delivers web push once the PWA is installed to the home screen (16.4+), so push reach on iPhone was тЙИ0. New `src/components/IOSInstallBanner.js` (mounted in `Layout.js`) self-gates to iOS Safari that hasn't installed тАФ renders `null` for Android/desktop/installed/iOS-Chrome, so zero blast radius elsewhere. Auto-shows on the 3rd app-open (per-session visit counter in localStorage) and immediately on a `rinkd:ios-install-prompt` event, which `Tournament.js handleFollowToggle` now dispatches when a user taps Follow and push is blocked тАФ replacing the old dead-end "enable from Profile" alert (which couldn't work pre-install on iOS anyway). Dismiss hides it 14 days. Analytics: `ios_install_banner_shown {trigger}` / `ios_install_banner_dismissed`. Detection extracted to `src/lib/platform.js` (`detectPlatform` / `detectStandalone` / `iosCanInstallButHasnt`) as the canonical source for new code; the inline copies in `InstallButton.js` / `DownloadCTA.js` left untouched. **Improvement over the parity spec:** gated to iOS *Safari* only (the spec used a naive `/iphone/` UA test) тАФ iOS Chrome/Firefox can't "Add to Home Screen", so prompting them would be wrong. **тЪая╕П Not browser-tested** тАФ an iOS-only banner doesn't render on desktop; needs one real-iPhone eyeball (open in Safari тЖТ tap Follow тЖТ confirm it slides up above the nav) before relying on it. Additive + dismissible, so low risk.

**GS-3 тАФ in-app game clock: HELD (not building).** Pete declined May 21. There's no data feed from arena scoreclock hardware (Daktronics/OES/etc.), so any in-app clock тАФ GS-3, GameSheet's, anyone's тАФ is an independent software clock the scorer runs manually. It can't track the real board (a hockey clock stops on every whistle; a scorer can't mirror that while recording events), so it drifts by minutes. A confident-but-wrong pre-filled `time_in_period` on the official record is worse than an empty field the scorer fills by glancing at the board. Revisit only if a venue staffs ONE person doing both scoreclock + scoresheet (then the app clock could *be* their clock). Captured in memory `feature-judgment-correctness-over-convenience`.

**Tape-job font on headers + wordmark (`f96c6d14`, `909d84d9`, `086cde2e`).** Pete's hand-made "tape job" alphabet specimen (`~/Downloads/Tapejob_font.png` тАФ AтАУZ uppercase, white athletic tape on black) sliced into 26 transparent glyph PNGs in `public/tapejob/` (grid auto-detected by pixel projection via Pillow, tight-cropped, blackтЖТalpha with the woven texture preserved). New `src/components/TapeText.js` renders any string from those glyphs: keeps the real text as `aria-label` (accessible + SEO-indexable; the `<img>`s are `aria-hidden`), upper-cases input, gaps spaces, and falls back to condensed Barlow for digits/punctuation (only AтАУZ glyphs exist). Applied to the **static section headers**: Feed (CHIRPS), Teams, Notifications, Tournaments, Leagues, Discover, Store. Composed a tape **RINKD wordmark** (`public/rinkd-wordmark-tape.png`) and pointed both wordmark refs at it тАФ the `RinkdLogo` lockup (desktop sidebar + mobile top bar) and the `Wordmark` component (Auth / Landing / ResetPassword heroes) тАФ plus the landing-page three-up brand strip and the survey page header (both hardcoded the old `/rinkd-wordmark.png` directly, bypassing the components). **Scope decisions:** Profile's header is the user's *dynamic* name тЖТ left in the regular font; **Rinkside skipped** (it has its own dedicated logo image, a sub-brand mark, not a text title); **SEO `og:image` deliberately left on `/rinkd-wordmark-large.png`** тАФ a transparent white wordmark would disappear on light social-share backgrounds (wants a proper opaque 1200├Ч630 card, separate task). Old `/rinkd-wordmark.png` + `/rinkd-wordmark-large.png` are now unused but kept (easy revert). **To add a new tape header:** `import TapeText`, wrap a short uppercase string, pass `height` (px) тАФ only ever scale DOWN from the ~200px source art. **тЪая╕П Verify on a real screen** тАФ esp. the Auth 140px hero (source art ~200px tall, so it may look slightly soft at that size; the grungy texture mostly hides it). Verified the glyph cutouts + header sizing via render previews during the build; the live in-app render still wants an eyeball.

**Event-page view tracking fixed (`5ec7067c`).** `tournament_public_view` / `league_public_view` had recorded **zero** since they shipped May 20 тАФ they fired only inside the anon `PublicTournamentLanding` / `PublicLeagueLanding` branch (`!currentUser`), but every real viewer (commissioner, team managers, signed-up fans) is logged in and never hits that branch. Moved the view event up to the top-level page component (`TournamentPage` / `LeaguePage`) so it fires for **every** visitor, now tagged with `{ anonymous: true|false }` (ref-guarded, once per page load). Total event-page interest is finally measurable; filter `anonymous=true` for share-driven/cold traffic. Rows should start accumulating once redeployed (gut-check in a day).

**Auth signup-default verified live (`9b50a41f`, shipped May 20).** May 21 traffic check: every auth-screen session that day opened in **signup** mode (vs 12 of 13 in *login* the day before) тАФ confirms the cold-traffic login-wall fix is working in prod. Conversion lift still TBD (sample too small + half-day). `login_failed` holding at ~0/day, so the Turnstile login fix remains stable.

**`/pricing` page shipped (`73fea303`).** Public `/pricing` page (anon-shareable + Google-indexable, standalone like `/survey`) rendering the locked ladders from `docs/Rinkd_Pricing_Guide.docx`: league tiers ($299/$599/$999 + $99 division add-on), tournament tiers ($149/$299/$499/$799), the league-member cross-sell (Yr1 free / Yr2+ 15% off), and the 1% registration fee. Tape "PRICING" header. BLPA intentionally absent (custom deal). Wired into the organizer conversion path тАФ **NOT a nav tab** (seller-facing, low-frequency): "See pricing" links on the Run-your-league / Host-your-tournament banners (`League.js` Info tab + `PublicTournamentLanding`), the Activation-pending banners (`TournamentManage` / `LeagueManage`), and a low-key row in `MoreDrawer`. New `src/pages/Pricing.js` + public route in `App.js`. No tier-enforcement dependency тАФ pure marketing asset. тЪая╕П Not visually verified from Claude Code тАФ wants a desktop + mobile eyeball.

**тЪая╕П Known flow gap (change-later, Pete May 21):** the pricing-page CTAs route into the **free** create wizard (`/league/create` / `/tournament/create`) тАФ there is no payment step, because today's model is create-free тЖТ configure тЖТ email `hello@rinkd.app` тЖТ Pete manually flips `is_activated` after out-of-band payment. Someone arriving via the pricing page has high purchase intent, so once Stripe ships (BIZ-INFRA-1 / LA-1 / TOURN-REG-1) the pricing CTAs should route into **checkout first**, not the bare wizard. Don't leave the free-wizard flow once payments exist. See memory `pricing-flow-needs-payment-gating` + the ┬з7 revenue note. Until Stripe lands, the free flow stands.

Built + live: `products` table (public-read RLS `products_select_active`, no client write policies тЖТ service-role/admin only, upsert key `(source, external_id)`), `src/lib/products.js`, rebuilt `src/pages/Store.js` (Rinkd-design cards, curated collection sections, affiliate click-out `rel="sponsored"` new-tab, **FTC affiliate disclosure**, "Pro Shop dropping soon" state), `store_view` + `store_product_click` analytics. **Scaffolded, NOT deployed:** `supabase/functions/sync-avantlink-products/index.ts` (fetch feed тЖТ upsert; returns `skipped` until `AVANTLINK_FEED_URL` set). **If Pure Hockey unblocks (merchant vouch or reapply):** get our affiliate/website ID + Pure Hockey merchant ID + the datafeed URL/format, fill the feed mapping (illustrative TODO now), set the secret, deploy + schedule a daily cron. **Rinkd merch is parked until Stripe** тАФ build it as native Printful+Stripe checkout, not the manual link-out. ### May 23, 2026 тАФ Stat leaderboards shipped (tournament + league) тАФ closes the GameSheet Players/Goalies gap

Triggered by BLPA sharing GameSheet screenshots (DEX tournament: Scores, Players, Goalies, Standings). Assessment: Rinkd was at/above parity on standings + box scores but had **no player/goalie leaderboards** тАФ the one real gap. Key insight: GameSheet's many extra columns (PPG/SHG/PP%/PK%/SOG/PPGAтАж) are **empty even in BLPA's own data** (the rec scorekeeper never logs PP/PK/EN situations), so effective parity only needs G/A/PTS/PIM (skaters) + GAA/SV%/record (goalies) тАФ all of which Rinkd already captures. Shipped a Phase-1 review-only **Stats tab** on both the Tournament (`3e1b57d2`) and League (`a2c7a9e3`) pages.

**Architecture тАФ 4 RPCs + 1 shared component, no schema change:**
- `get_tournament_skater_stats(p_tournament_id)` / `get_tournament_goalie_stats(p_tournament_id)` and `get_league_skater_stats(p_league_id)` / `get_league_goalie_stats(p_league_id)`. All **SECURITY INVOKER**, granted `anon, authenticated` (every backing table is public-select). Applied to prod via MCP (additive; unused until the frontend shipped).
- `src/components/StatLeaderboards.js` тАФ shared component, `source` prop (`'tournament'|'league'`) picks the RPC pair. Skaters board (GP/G/A/PTS/PIM/Pt-G) + Goalies board (GP/W-L-T/GA/SA/SV%/GAA/SO), Skaters/Goalies toggle, loading/error/empty states. Added as a `Stats` tab on `Tournament.js` (`Standings┬╖Schedule┬╖Bracket┬╖Stats┬╖Feed┬╖Info`) and `League.js` (`Schedule┬╖Standings┬╖Stats┬╖Teams┬╖Feed┬╖Info`). Replaced the initial tournament-only `TournamentStats.js`.

**Data model (verified, not assumed):**
- **Tournament:** stat rows key on `tournament_teams.id` (`game_goals.team_id` = `games.home/away_team_id` = `tournament_teams.id`). Names from `game_lineups.invite_name` (fallback `profiles.name/handle`, then `#jersey`). Goalie-of-record = `game_lineups.is_goalie=true`; SA from opponent `game_shots` + the goalie's games; GA from goal log; GAA per-game; SV% null when no shots. Validated against a synthetic finalized game (inserted + rolled back; BLPA never touched) тАФ every number exact.
- **League:** stat rows key on `league_teams.id` (`game_goals.team_id` = `league_games.home/away_team_id` = `league_teams.id`). **League games have NO `game_lineups`**, so names come from `team_members` via `league_teams.team_id тЖТ team_members(team_id, jersey_number)`. Team name = `coalesce(teams.name, league_teams.team_name)` (the latter is anon-readable even when `teams.is_public=false`). **Goalie board is per-TEAM goaltending** тАФ league games don't record who was in net (`game_goalie_changes` is essentially unused, 1 row), so GA comes from final scores, SA from opponent `game_shots`, and the line is attributed to the roster goalie (`team_members.position='Goalie'`) **only when a team has exactly one**, else `"<Team> (goaltending)"`. Validated against **Demo Beer League**: skater names resolve 86/86, GAA/record/SO correct, W-L-T reconciles to 15 games. (KOHA itself has no scored games yet тЖТ empty state until played.)

**Decisions/notes:**
- **Login-gated by design (Pete, May 23): keep it gated тАФ maximize sign-ups.** The Stats tab sits inside the signed-in tabbed view on both pages, exactly where standings already live; anon visitors get the sign-up teaser landing (`PublicTournamentLanding` / `PublicLeagueLanding`). This **revises** the original ┬з7 KOHA-parity note that assumed "League.js, already anon-public" тАФ it is NOT; live data (standings/schedule/stats) requires sign-in, deliberately. Do NOT surface stats on the public landing without a fresh Pete decision (it weakens the conversion forcing-function).
- Goalies excluded from the skater board via an `is_goalie` flag on the skater RPC.
- **P% column added to tournament standings** (client-side, `pts/(gp├Чpoints_win)`). League standings left as-is (fixed CSS grid; P% would crowd mobile).
- Index hygiene pass at the same time: every leaderboard join/filter path was already covered by existing indexes (`game_id` on all stat tables, `tournament_id`/`status` on games, `user_id` on lineups). Found + fixed the only real gap тАФ 4 unindexed FKs on `team_manager_invites` (migration `fk_indexes_team_manager_invites`) тАФ restoring advisor `unindexed_foreign_keys` тЖТ **0**. Remaining advisor noise unchanged: 39 unused indexes (expected pre-traffic), 100 `multiple_permissive_policies` (the known post-pilot RLS-cleanup backlog).
- **Phase-1 follow-ups not built:** penalty-by-type board, phase-split (reg vs playoff), division-split, and тАФ for true league *per-goalie* GAA/SV% тАФ capturing goalie-in-net during league scoring. Phase 2 = tie jersey stats to profiles once players sign up (`link_invited_player`). See memory `stat-leaderboards`.

### May 23, 2026 тАФ Auto-follow seed accounts changed to Pete + BLPA + Howie

Pete found that new signups were auto-following the `@demo.rinkd.app` demo accounts. Root cause: TWO mechanisms тАФ the `tr_auto_follow_pete` DB trigger (Pete only) + a client-side block in `ensureProfileForUser` (`src/lib/auth.js`) that followed the **top 3 profiles by `points`** (which were the demo accounts). Consolidated into one server-side trigger and removed the client block (`8eac422e`).

- **Migration `auto_follow_seed_accounts_pete_blpa_howie`:** new function `auto_follow_seed_accounts_on_profile_insert()` (SECURITY DEFINER) loops `['pete@rinkd.app','nick@blpa.com','howard@cemented.ca']`, looks each up by `lower(profiles.email)`, inserts a follow (skip self, on-conflict-nothing). New trigger `tr_auto_follow_seed_accounts`; dropped old `tr_auto_follow_pete` + its function. So every new account follows **Pete (@Pete) + The BLPA (@TheBLPA) + Howie Miller (@Howitzer, KOHA commissioner)**.
- **`src/lib/auth.js`:** removed the "follow top 3 by points" block (the demo-seed source). Trigger is now the single source of truth.
- **Migration `backfill_real_user_seed_follows_pete_blpa_howie`:** for the 14 real (non-demo, non-seed) users тАФ deleted demo-account follows (38 rows) + added the 3 seed follows (27 rows). Disabled `trg_notify_on_follow` during the backfill so the seed accounts weren't hit with a burst of "followed you" notifications, then re-enabled. Verified 0 real users still follow a demo account.
- **тЪая╕П Still open (parked, Pete's call):** onboarding step-2 "suggested players" (`OnboardingModal.js`) still surfaces top-by-points = demo accounts for *manual* follow. The last spot a real user sees demo profiles тАФ pre-launch cleanup. Memory `auto-follow-seed-accounts`.

### ~~ЁЯФ┤ Forgot-password flow~~ тАФ тЬЕ FIXED May 18, 2026 morning

**Root cause (now resolved):** The Supabase reset email's `redirect_to` was `https://www.rinkd.app` (Site URL fallback), NOT `https://rinkd.app/reset-password` that the app sends. The allowlist rejected the apex redirect because the apex domain wasn't permitted. **0 users had ever successfully completed a password reset** in production prior to this fix (including BLPA Nick on May 14 тАФ his recovery token was never consumed).

**Fix applied (Supabase Dashboard тЖТ Authentication тЖТ URL Configuration):**
- Site URL changed `https://www.rinkd.app` тЖТ `https://rinkd.app`
- Redirect URLs added: `https://rinkd.app/reset-password`, `https://rinkd.app/*`, `https://www.rinkd.app/*`, `http://localhost:3000/*`

**E2E verified May 18, 13:39 UTC:** Pete completed full Forgot Password тЖТ email тЖТ click тЖТ set new password тЖТ land on `/feed` flow. DB confirmed: `last_sign_in_at` = 2026-05-18 13:39:51, `still_unused` = false, `updated_at` = 2026-05-18 13:40:06. `ResetPassword.js` listener race did NOT manifest тАФ no defensive patch needed.

**BLPA captains can now reset their passwords** if they hit the flow during pilot onboarding.

- **Supabase тЖТ Authentication тЖТ Policies тЖТ "Leaked password protection"** тАФ flip ON. HaveIBeenPwned integration, blocks compromised passwords on signup/reset. Pure upside, one toggle.

### May 31, 2026 тАФ Feed + social polish (8 ships, all on `main`)

A social-layer cleanup pass plus two engagement features for BLPA. All eight shipped + pushed to `main`; every build clean except the pre-existing "Critical dependency" warning (from a dependency, not our code).

- **MENTION-1 wire-in finished + merged** (`c2d15689`, branch `feature/mentions-and-scoped-likes` тЖТ `main`). @-mention tagging is now live in **every** composer тАФ global Feed, TeamFeed, League `LeagueFeedTab`, Tournament `FeedTab`, and all comment boxes тАФ via `MentionInput` (autocomplete) + `MentionText` (linkify). Resolved user-ids are stored in `post_mentions` / `comment_mentions` at create time; we never regex display text to decide who was mentioned (prevents notify-a-stranger + ambiguous-handle mis-links). Notifications fire from AFTER-INSERT triggers on the mention tables. `mention` added to notifications `KIND_META`. Push notifications for mentions were **deferred** (Pete: "leave it for now").
- **Like-count fix on league + tournament feeds** (`79f81aa8`). Likes never incremented the visible count on those two feeds. Root cause: the optimistic `onLike` mutated a `nextLiked` var inside the `setLikedPosts` functional updater and read it back inside the `setPosts` updater. That ordering only holds when both pieces of state are local to one component (TeamFeed). On League/Tournament, `posts` is a **parent-owned prop**, so the parent's count updater flushed *first* and read a still-null `nextLiked`. Fixed by computing `const willLike = !likedPosts.includes(postId)` synchronously before any setState, and keying the liked-state `useEffect` on the post-id SET (`posts.map(p=>p.id).join(',')` via a ref) so it refetches when the list changes. Verified the DB layer was already consistent тАФ `posts.likes` is maintained by `bump_post_like_count()` AFTER INSERT/DELETE triggers; no data repair needed.
- **Team-scoped posts kept OUT of the global Chirp feed** (`b0f32fec`). `getPosts` (Discover) + `getFollowingPosts` (Following) already filtered `tournament_id`/`league_id` to NULL but not `team_id`, so one team post was leaking into the global feed. Added `.is('team_id', null)` to both. Pete's explicit choice (AskUserQuestion): team posts live on the team feed only.
- **Authors can delete their own posts + comments** (`18bf2fad`). Previously there was no delete UI (DB/RLS already allowed it). `PostActionMenu` now branches on ownership: own content тЖТ ЁЯЧС Delete (with a `window.confirm` whose copy differs for post vs comment); others' content тЖТ the existing Report + Block. New `deletePost(postId)` / `deleteComment(commentId)` in `lib/posts.js` (thin `.delete().eq('id', тАж)` тАФ RLS `posts_delete_own` / `comments_delete_own` enforce author-only). Deleting a **post** cascades its `comments`, `likes`, `notifications`, and `post_mentions` (all FKs `ON DELETE CASCADE`); deleting a single **comment** removes only that comment and its `comment_mentions`, and `posts.comment_count` self-corrects because `trg_bump_post_comment_count` fires on DELETE too. Wired the `onDeleted` callback through Feed, TeamFeed, League, and Tournament (parent removes the row + adjusts counts).
- **LiveBarn Venue ID input removed from the global Feed composer** (`35221339`). The optional free-text "ЁЯУ║ LiveBarn Venue ID" field asked casual posters to paste a raw numeric venue id тАФ poor UX and redundant with the per-game/league stream-URL plumbing (`youtube_url`, `src/lib/streamUrl.js`). Dropped the input, its `livebarnId` state, the `setLivebarnId` reset, and the `livebarn` analytics flag, and stopped passing `livebarnVenueId` to `createPost`. **Kept** the render-side "ЁЯУ║ Watch Live on LiveBarn" deep-link (Feed.js ~196-198) so any existing posts with a `livebarn_venue_id` still render the button тАФ reversible, leaves old data intact.
- **URL autolinking in posts, comments, AND profile bios** (`a653ae0a`). `MentionText` (`src/components/Mentions.js`) now linkifies explicit `http(s)://` and `www.` URLs alongside @handles. It collects both token types, sorts by position, and walks the text in one **overlap-guarded** left-to-right pass (an `@` sitting inside a URL won't double-match). URLs render as `<a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow ugc">` (user content тАФ safe, no SEO juice); trailing sentence punctuation (`.`, `)`, `,`, тАж) is peeled off the href and re-emitted as text; `www.` gets `https://` prepended. **Bare `foo.com` stays plain on purpose** (avoids mislinking handles/prices). Profile bios (Profile.js ~406) now route through `MentionText text={profile.bio} mentions={{}}`. Posts/comments inherited URL linking automatically since they already used `MentionText`. **Known gap:** the bio *edit* field has no live link preview тАФ users see styling only after save.
- **Emoji reactions on posts across all feeds** (`fbc843d2`, REACT-1). An additive layer **alongside** the existing тЭдя╕П like тАФ the like / `posts.likes` plumbing (and its `bump_post_like_count` triggers) is untouched. New `post_reactions` table (RLS mirrors `likes`; one row per `(post_id, user_id, emoji)`); counts are aggregated on **read** (no denormalized column, no trigger) and batched one query per visible page via `getReactions(userId, postIds)` тЖТ `{ [postId]: { [emoji]: { count, mine } } }`. Shared `<PostReactions postId currentUserId initial>` renders a pill strip over the curated set ЁЯФеЁЯЪиЁЯШВЁЯеЕЁЯТкЁЯН║ plus a я╝Л picker popover (outside-click/Esc closes). The component owns its optimistic state seeded from `initial`; **toggle is its own inverse**, so a failed write rolls back by re-applying the same toggle. Wired into Feed, TeamFeed, League `LeagueFeedTab`, and Tournament `FeedTab`; logged-out viewers see read-only pills (no picker, no toggling).
- **Photo/video gallery on Tournament + League pages** (`331f5d4c`, GALLERY-1). A media-only grid **over scoped posts** тАФ deliberately **not** a new table тАФ so every photo inherits reactions/comments/likes/moderation for free. `src/components/Gallery.js` is self-contained: pass exactly one of `tournamentId` / `leagueId` and it loads its own competing-team list + media posts. New **Gallery** tab added to both `Tournament` TABS and `League` TABS. Header = team **filter chips** (All + one per competing team) and a dedicated **"Add Photo"** CTA opening a modal (photo/video picker w/ preview + optional caption + optional team tag тЖТ `uploadMedia` then scoped `createPost`); tapping a thumbnail opens a **lightbox** with the caption, author, scoped-team badge, and inline `<PostReactions>`. **Data model:** tournament/league competing teams live in their own tables (`tournament_teams` / `league_teams`), **not** the global `teams` table, so team-tagging needed per-scope columns rather than reusing `posts.team_id` (which is the team's own TeamFeed scope and would cross-contaminate it). Added nullable `posts.tournament_team_id` тЖТ `tournament_teams(id)` and `posts.league_team_id` тЖТ `league_teams(id)`, both `ON DELETE SET NULL` with partial indexes. `getGalleryPosts({ tournamentId|leagueId, tournamentTeamId|leagueTeamId, limit })` returns `media_url is not null` + `is_hidden=false` posts for the scope, embedding profiles + the scoped team for labeling. `createPost` gained `tournamentTeamId` / `leagueTeamId` params. No standalone post route exists, so the lightbox shows reactions inline (no "view post" link).

---

### June 1, 2026 тАФ 1:1 DMs, social push pipeline, live game strip, mobile-nav polish + Game Puck fan vote (8 ships, all on `main`)
- **1:1 Direct messages** (`bc98fa30`) тАФ `conversations` + `conversation_participants` + `messages` tables, RLS scoped to participants, `get_or_create_dm(p_other)` RPC (returns a uuid, throws on error). `/messages` inbox + `/messages/:id` thread (`src/pages/Messages.js`), client lib `src/lib/messages.js`. Mobile inbox icon (`MessagesIcon`) sits in the top-right bar to the LEFT of the bell. Blocks are respected (no DM either direction). Push reuses the notifications pipeline via hidden `kind='message'` notification rows.
- **Social push loop + live game strip** (`be6aa01e`) тАФ Tournament Feed renders a live game strip showing **PERIOD ONLY** (`period_time` is a dead/unreliable column тАФ do NOT surface a clock). Web push now fires on comment / mention / reaction via an AFTER-INSERT trigger on `notifications` тЖТ `pg_net` тЖТ the generic `send-notification-push` edge function (gated in the trigger WHEN clause). New reaction-notify trigger; `reaction` added to `KIND_META`. Verified end-to-end.
- **DM mobile composer fix** (`d0e2a06e`) тАФ the thread is now a `position:fixed` panel sized between the mobile top bar (52px) and bottom nav (`calc(88px + safe-area)`), with the message list as the only internal scroll (`flex:1; min-height:0; overflow-y:auto`) and the composer pinned (`flex-shrink:0`). So the text field is always on-screen тАФ no more scrolling to type. HelpButton is hidden on `/messages/:id` routes (`useLocation` regex) so the floating "?" stops covering the Send button.
- **Message button on user profiles** (`0e169f79`) тАФ `src/pages/Profile.js` gained a ЁЯТм Message button (only on others' profiles) that calls `getOrCreateDm(profileId)` then `navigate('/messages/:id')`; fires `dm_opened_from_profile` analytics.
- **Profile action-row wrap fix** (`242aeea6`) тАФ adding Message made the Block/Message/Follow row overflow off-screen on narrow phones (flex nowrap). Fixed with `flexWrap:'wrap'` + `justifyContent:'flex-end'` on both the cluster and button-group divs. Block was never removed in code тАФ it was just pushed out of the viewport.
- **Mobile bottom nav тЖТ 4 items** (`575e3349`) тАФ dropped the redundant Notifications bell from the mobile bottom bar (it already lives top-right next to Messages). `Layout.js`: `const MOBILE_NAV = NAV.filter(item => item.path !== '/notifications')`; mobile bottom bar maps `MOBILE_NAV`, the desktop sidebar still maps the full `NAV` (no top bar on desktop, so it keeps the bell).
- **Webhook-miss recovery** (`05f1310e`) тАФ production was stuck because Vercel's GitHub webhook silently dropped a push (`242aeea6`). The Vercel MCP tools are read-only (can't create a deploy), so an empty `git commit --allow-empty` re-fired the webhook and the build went READY. **Recurring gotcha тАФ see ┬з9.** Reminder for users: the PWA service worker caches aggressively, so a deploy only shows after a hard-refresh / app reopen.
- **Rinkd Game Puck тАФ fan "Fans' Pick" vote** (SOCIAL-3 Phase 1, `d2ec605b` on `main`) тАФ fan vote for the player of the game on **FINAL** league + tournament games. **Jersey-keyed** (rosters are thin / tournament teams are nameplate-only тАФ same pattern as stat leaderboards): candidate players = game lineup тИк goal-log participants. **One vote per user per game, change-able; winner computed on read** (no denormalized counts). NO push / NO auto-post in Phase 1 (deferred fast-follow). DB: `game_puck_votes` (polymorphic `game_id` XOR `league_game_id` + matching team ref via CHECK; `unique(voter_id, game_id)` + `unique(voter_id, league_game_id)`) + RLS (open read to authenticated, insert-own-only-on-`status='final'`, update/delete own) + 3 SECURITY-INVOKER RPCs `cast_game_puck_vote` / `get_game_puck` / `get_season_game_pucks` (anon-granted reads). UI: `GamePuckCard` in `GameDetail` (live tally + leader + tap-to-vote chips, login-gated) + `SeasonGamePucks` board in the League **and** Tournament Stats tabs (pucks won per team+jersey across the season, hidden until first vote). Client lib `src/lib/gamePucks.js`. Migration applied to prod via MCP (repo doesn't track local migration files); DB-verified end-to-end (tally + season argmax); zero new advisor warnings. **Not yet browser-tested.**

### June 2, 2026 тАФ Scorer tap-to-log + Chirp engagement polish (2 ships, all on `main`)
- **`SCORER-TAP-1` тАФ tap a team / score to log a goal** (`c54ff751`, merged `d932416c`). From the Jun 1 Nick (BLPA) call тАФ timekeepers are 10тАУ70 yrs old, wants goal entry stupid-proof. In `src/pages/ScorerView.js` (shared component тЖТ tournament **and** league at once) the team name (now carrying a "+ Goal" pill) and the big score number are tap targets that open the Log Goal form prefilled to that side. Non-destructive: opening writes nothing, Save confirms, тЬХ undoes. **`+` now opens the Log Goal form too (Jun 2 fix `ee01bfc3`)** тАФ it was a silent raw-score bump that confused even Pete, so a 10тАУ70yo timekeeper would've too, and it let the raw score drift from the goal log; routing it through the form keeps them in sync. `тИТ` stays as the quick score-correction escape hatch (the `changePeriod` final-guard just compares score vs goal log, unaffected). Pure client, no schema/RLS. тЪая╕П Still wants a real-iPad eyeball (PRE-5) тАФ confirm the tap targets feel right on hardware.
- **`FEED-ENGAGE-1` тАФ Chirp feed engagement polish** (`a5688c53`, merged `d932416c`). Two UX wins on the global feed (`src/pages/Feed.js` + `src/components/PostReactions.js`): (1) **rotating chirp starters** тАФ the composer prompt cycles through hockey / beer-league prompts every ~4s while collapsed (crossfade; pauses while composing; the showing prompt becomes the ghost text; respects `prefers-reduced-motion`); (2) **reaction pop** тАФ tapping a reaction springs the emoji + lofts a ghost copy up/away (add-only, not on remove). Keyframes injected once per page (the app styles inline, no global stylesheet). Pure client, no schema. **Shelved feed ideas (Pete, Jun 2):** a "Live Now" cross-platform game strip (best right before the BLPA weekend) + a "Hot" trending-chirp tab.

#### A. GROWTH-SHARE-1 тАФ COMPLETE + LIVE on `main` (the zero-CAC sharing loop)
The loop runs on prod: tap Share on a recap/Game-Puck/photo тЖТ branded image composed **client-side** (canvas, zero server cost) тЖТ native share sheet on mobile / download+copy-link modal on desktop тЖТ deep-links to a **login-less public page** тЖТ and a **pasted link unfurls the branded card** (per-game OG). Commits on `main`:

- **`993df4d6`** desktop Share fix (`prefersNativeShare` тАФ desktop always gets the modal, mobile gets the native sheet) + Share button on the in-app GameDetail page.
- **`1091c672`** Merge **M4** OG unfurl тАФ `middleware.js` (Vercel **Edge Middleware**, runs on CRA; matcher `/g`,`/lg`; UA-sniffs crawlers тЖТ per-game OG HTML, humans тЖТ SPA passthrough, no redirect) + `og:image` = the stored client card (`share-cards/<g|lg>/<id>.png`) if present, else `/og-fallback-rinkd.png` (1200├Ч630, committed). `src/lib/ogCard.js` = fire-and-forget wide-card upload **on authed share** (anon can't write тЖТ a game's OG upgrades fallbackтЖТreal card after the **first signed-in share**). `share-cards` public bucket + RLS live on prod. **Verified via curl on prod** (botтЖТOG tags, humanтЖТSPA, coldтЖТfallback, uploadedтЖТstored card).

Audit work is **done**. The post-audit landscape, in priority order:

### June 8, 2026 тАФ Monetization + Growth build (XRHL + Little Caesars driven) тАФ SPEC'd, build target post-pilot / late June
Three specs landed Jun 8 (all in `rinkd_v4/`). This is the **next major build push after the BLPA pilot.** Driven by the XRHL deal (Adam Stio тАФ sponsor monetization is his #1 ask) and the Little Caesars Summer Sizzle (Brennan Gerbe, Aug 1 тАФ family/under-13 profiles committed on the call).

1. **`ADS-1` тАФ League/team-page advertising** тАФ spec: `rinkd_v4/Rinkd_Ad_Placements_Spec.md`. Self-served sponsor inventory on league/team pages (banner, "presented by" lockups on standings/schedule, native feed unit, **recap sponsor = highest value**, Game Puck sponsor). **Zero fixed cost:** admins upload their own creative; serve from existing Supabase storage/CDN; client-side weighted rotation; lightweight impression/tap counts (`ad_creatives` / `ad_placements` / `ad_events`). **Inventory boundary (hold firm):** their pages = their sponsors, **they keep 100% in yr1**; global Rinkd spaces = Rinkd's (yr2 network inventory + rev share). Framing = the "digital dasher board." Fan-experience caps: no interstitials/popups/autoplay; "presented by" over banner-blasting. Youth: no behavioral targeting on minors.

2. **`GROWTH-SHARE-1` тАФ Native sharing + the growth loop** тАФ spec: `rinkd_v4/Rinkd_Growth_Sharing_Spec.md`. **THE zero-CAC distribution engine.** Share button on **recaps, Game Puck / Player-of-Game cards, gallery photos** тЖТ pre-composed **branded image** via client-side **canvas** тЖТ **Web Share API** (`navigator.share({files})`) one-tap to IG/iMessage/X (desktop fallback: download + copy link). Every share **deep-links back to a login-less public page** + soft install prompt; **Open Graph tags** on every public entity so a pasted link also unfurls a branded preview (image OR link, both branded). Recap share-card = dual-brand zones: **sponsor top strip, Rinkd frame bottom strip, never shared; Rinkd mark un-croppable; locked template** (recognizability is the asset). Youth guardrails: minor Player-of-Game cards parent/account-controlled, COPPA-aware. **P1 ship (turns on the loop):** share button + recap card + Web Share API + OG/login-less public pages. **P2:** Game Puck card (most viral тАФ pulls the player's family graph) + gallery watermark + shareтЖТvisitтЖТinstall funnel metrics. *Pairs with `ADS-1` тАФ the recap/Game-Puck sponsor lockups are the intersection.*

3. **`FAMILY-1` тАФ Family/parent profiles (under-13) + game RSVP** (committed on the Little Caesars call Jun 8; ~1тАУ2 wk). Parents create linked family profiles to **manage players under 13** + **RSVP/attendance** per game. Serves youth orgs (LC, MHT-class); realizes the `ARCH-DUAL-1` youth skin. COPPA-sensitive тАФ players under 13 are managed by the parent account, not their own login.

4. **`XRHL-MIRROR-1` тАФ HockeyShift live mirror for XRHL** тАФ **тЬЕ AUTHORIZED in writing Jun 8** (Adam Stio: "we approve you to mirror the site"). Free year-1 trial; his directors are evaluating. Mirror XRHL's HockeyShift game data into the league hub (the `SOCIAL-2` poller pattern). League: "eXtreme Roller Hockey League" (id `a1b2c3d4-e5f6-7890-abcd-ef1234567890`), Summer 2026, Huntington Center, Toledo. Directors onboarding as admins (Brydon Frisk signed up; Dorreon Floyd pending) тАФ added via manual `commissioner`-role SQL until `LEAGUE-MGR-1` ships. тЪая╕П **Watch item / year-1 upsell:** Adam engaged the native Score View unprompted тАФ if XRHL scores **natively in Rinkd**, they become a real platform customer AND it **erases the HockeyShift authorization/ToS dependency entirely.** Plant via a scrimmage/opener trial; don't push.

5. **`LEAGUE-MGR-1` тАФ league-level staff/manager roles + UI** (surfaced Jun 8 by the XRHL onboarding). **Gap:** there is NO way to add a league-level admin/manager in the app тАФ LeagueManage has Teams/Divisions/Schedule/Playoffs/Registrations/Settings but no "Staff/Managers" screen, and `league_roles` only contains the `commissioner` role (no lesser tier). So onboarding a director (e.g. XRHL's Dorreon Floyd / Brydon Frisk) today requires a manual `INSERT INTO league_roles (...) role='commissioner'` via SQL тАФ which grants FULL commissioner power including delete-the-league. **Build:** (1) a real `manager` role (manage feed/teams/schedule/gallery, **cannot** delete the league or change billing) checked by `is_league_commissioner`'s sibling `is_league_manager`; (2) a Staff/Managers section in LeagueManage тЖТ Settings to add/remove by email/handle (mirror the team-manager flow + the `IDENT-1`/identity discipline тАФ link-on-verified-account, never auto-create); (3) RLS so a manager can't escalate themselves or others. Pairs with the FAMILY-1 / permissions work. Until built, league-director onboarding = manual commissioner-role SQL (trusted directors only).

**Infra cost guardrails (Jun 8 тАФ model: `rinkd_v4/Rinkd_Infra_Scaling_Model.xlsx`).** Cost scales with PHOTOS + ENGAGEMENT, not signups тАФ even ~50 leagues / ~42k users тЙИ **~$48/mo** (Supabase Pro + Vercel Pro + a few $ email), PROVIDED these four design rules hold. Build them in from the start; they constrain `GROWTH-SHARE-1` (push/share), the email work, and any live-game feature:
1. **Push fan-out MUST be batched** тАФ one edge-function invocation loops out to ALL subscribers of an event, never one-invocation-per-recipient. Unbatched, a single league's goal-alerts (~330k/season) blows the free 500k edge cap at ~1.5 leagues. Web Push/FCM itself is free; the cost is invocations.
2. **Push for engagement, email for transactional only** тАФ email is the only real per-message cost AND the rate-limited/deliverability-sensitive channel. (Reinforces `EMAILVERIFY-1`: Supabase built-in SMTP is test-only; wire Resend/SES on a `rinkd.com` domain with SPF/DKIM. SES new accounts start in a 200/day sandbox тАФ request production early.)
3. **Images тЖТ Cloudflare R2** when storage/egress climbs (zero egress fees; $0.015/GB). Photos are the first ceiling тАФ ~a dozen photo-heavy leagues exceed the 1GB free storage. Share-card images are composed client-side (canvas), so they cost nothing; uploaded gallery photos + OG previews are the driver.
4. **Live scoring: cache the score, passive viewers POLL a CDN value** тАФ reserve realtime sockets for active scorers only. Realtime cap is 200 free / 500 Pro concurrent; socket-per-viewer hits it on one hot game. A 2,000-fan game = ~2 connections, not 2,000.

- **MENTION-1 тАФ @-mention / user tagging in posts + comments** (~3-5 days; Pete, May 27). Today there is NO user tagging тАФ `posts.tag` is a *category label* ("Game Recap"), and `@handle` only ever appears as display text; no autocomplete, no mention storage, no notification. Build: (1) **composer @-autocomplete** тАФ type `@` тЖТ debounced profile search by handle+name (reuse the Discover / `resolveProfile` search) тЖТ insert. (2) **Store resolved mentions at create time, do NOT regex display text** тАФ new `post_mentions(post_id тЖТ posts, mentioned_user_id тЖТ profiles, created_at)` (+ `comment_mentions`); content keeps a durable token so a later handle change doesn't break the link. (3) **Render** `@handle` as a tappable link to `/profile/:id`. (4) **Notify** each tagged user (new `mention` notification + optional push тАФ high-engagement moment; reuse the notification+push pipeline). **Guardrails:** respect `user_blocks` (no notify if blocked either way), suppress self-mention, **cap N mentions/post** (anti-spam), index `post_mentions(mentioned_user_id, created_at desc)` for a future "tagged you" view. Surfaces: global feed + team/league/tournament feeds + comments.
