Guardrails: respect `user_blocks`, suppress when the winner can't be resolved to a user, cap auto-posts to one/game.
- **`NAV-PIN-1` тАФ league quick-nav pin (тЬЕ SHIPPED + LIVE тАФ League-only v1, Jun 2; commits `46567618` + `421284ca`, eyeballed live on mobile).** Pete scoped v1 to **League only** (team pin = v2). A player's own league was reachable only via the **More drawer** (`MoreDrawer.js` тЖТ `/leagues` *directory*, not their actual league) or a Discover search. New `LeaguePinIcon` surfaces the user's league as a one-tap shortcut: the **league logo as a circular avatar** (falls back to accent/logo color + initials), tap тЖТ `/league/:id`. **Renders in two spots:** mobile top-right cluster, leftmost (left of Messages тАФ `Layout.js` ~248) and the desktop sidebar as a "My League" row under the brand. **"My league" is auto-derived** (zero-config тАФ no explicit pin UI in v1) by `getMyPrimaryLeague(userId)` in `src/lib/leagues.js`, first match wins: (1) a league I run (`leagues.commissioner_id`, then `league_roles` commissioner), (2) the league my team plays in (`team_members` тЖТ `league_teams`), (3) a league I follow (`league_subscriptions`). Fail-soft тЖТ no pin if none / on error. **Session-cached** at module level (Layout remounts per route since pages wrap their own `<Layout>`, so without the cache it'd be тЙд4 queries per nav). Renders nothing while resolving or if the user has no league. **Files:** `src/components/LeaguePinIcon.js` (new), `src/lib/leagues.js` (`getMyPrimaryLeague`), `src/components/Layout.js` (import + 2 mount points). Build compiles clean; **eyeballed live on mobile (Pete, Jun 2) тАФ looks good.** Avatar bumped 26тЖТ30px (`421284ca`). **v2 (deferred):** team pin too, explicit ЁЯУМ "Pin to nav" override on the league/team header, multiple/reorderable pins, clear-on-delete. NOT pilot-blocking.
- **`ANALYTICS-PAGEVIEW-1` тАФ global pageview tracking + 90d retention + top-pages reporting (тЬЕ SHIPPED + LIVE, Jun 2; commit `bf6acb92` + migration `analytics_pageview_rollup_prune_and_top_pages`).** Pilot data-collection ask (Pete, Jun 2). **Before:** analytics was hand-instrumented (~60 events), NO blanket pageview тАФ `trackPage` was defined but never called, so most app pages (Feed/Teams/Profile/Standings/Stats/ScorerView/etc.) emitted no view and in-app navigation paths couldn't be reconstructed. **Now:** `RouteAnalytics` (mounted inside the Router in `App.js`) fires a `page_view` on every route change; since `session_id` + `created_at` are already on every event, per-session clickstreams reconstruct via `ORDER BY created_at` within a session. `trackPage` records the **bare pathname (query string stripped)** so single-use tokens in invite/reset links never land in `analytics_events`. **Retention / free-tier cost:** `analytics_daily` + `analytics_dau` are PLAIN VIEWS over `analytics_events` (they recompute from raw, so a prune would erase their history) тАФ so added a persisted `analytics_daily_rollup` table (read RLS = commissioners/admins) + a daily pg_cron job `rinkd-analytics-maintenance-daily` (08:30 UTC) that rolls up the trailing 3d **then** prunes raw events older than 90d. Keeps the free-tier DB bounded (was **25.5 / 500 MB**; a weekend of pilot pageviews adds ~25тАУ120 MB тАФ comfortably under). **Reporting:** 2 `security_invoker` views (`analytics_top_pages`, `analytics_entry_pages`) + a new "Top pages ┬╖ last 30d" panel on `/admin/analytics` (path ┬╖ views ┬╖ sessions ┬╖ users). **Files:** `src/components/RouteAnalytics.js` (new), `src/lib/analytics.js` (`track` urlOverride + `trackPage` scrub + `loadTopPages`), `src/App.js` (mount), `src/pages/AdminAnalytics.js` (panel). Compiles clean; **pageview insert + panel verify on prod** (tracking is localhost-disabled by design + the panel is admin-gated). **Future:** a per-session path UI (today = ad-hoc SQL), a `(session_id, created_at)` index if reconstruction queries get heavy, and a persisted-rollup loader if Pete wants >30d DAU history. NOT pilot-blocking тАФ but it's the pilot's observability backbone.
- **`DIR-MOD-1` тАФ director / commissioner can hide posts in their own event (тЬЕ SHIPPED + LIVE, Jun 2; commit `a3d6d216` + migration `dir_mod_1_set_post_and_comment_hidden_rpcs`; RPC verified on prod тАФ non-director denied, real director allowed + flag flips, both rolled back).** **Gap (now closed):** there is NO per-event feed moderation today тАФ `PostActionMenu` offers Delete only to the post's author; everyone else gets Report/Block; only Rinkd staff (`/admin/moderation`, `is_admin`) can act, and that's platform-wide. A tournament director / league commissioner **cannot remove an abusive or off-topic post in their own event** тАФ a real pilot-credibility gap, and the thing that makes the "directors control the feed" sales line actually true (surfaced by the Jun 2 feed-accuracy review). **Mechanism is mostly already built:** `posts.is_hidden` exists and EVERY feed query filters `.eq('is_hidden', false)` (global / following / tournament / league / team / gallery тАФ `posts.js` lines 16/58/77/95/202/225), so a moderate action is just a flip of that flag тАФ the post drops from every feed instantly. **Build:** (1) **SECURITY DEFINER RPC** `set_post_hidden(p_post_id uuid, p_hidden bool)` тАФ **fail-closed**; resolve the post's scope server-side and allow ONLY if `is_tournament_director(post.tournament_id, auth.uid())` OR `is_league_commissioner(post.league_id, auth.uid())` OR `is_admin` (mirror the `admin_delete_*` gating; `posts` UPDATE stays locked down per FEAT-2, so go through the RPC, never a broad policy). (2) **Soft-hide, reversible** тАФ set `is_hidden=true` (NOT delete) so Rinkd staff can review/undo and a director can't permanently destroy content; add `hidden_by uuid` + `hidden_at timestamptz` for accountability (or a `moderation_actions` audit row). (3) **UI** тАФ a "ЁЯЩИ Hide post" item in `PostActionMenu` shown on others' posts when the viewer can moderate that post's scope (new `canModerate` prop from the active tournament/league role); optimistic remove from local state in the tournament + league FeedTabs. (4) optional: a director "Hidden posts" review list in TournamentManage / LeagueManage to unhide. **Guardrails:** the RPC re-checks scope and ignores any client-claimed role (a director must never hide posts outside their event); respect existing block/report. **тЪая╕П Regression + hotfix (Jun 2):** the first cut added `posts.hidden_by REFERENCES profiles(id)` тАФ a SECOND postsтЖТprofiles FK alongside `author_id` тАФ which made the bare `profiles(...)` embed in every feed query ambiguous and **errored all feeds platform-wide (blank feed for everyone, not just new users)**. Fixed by migration `dir_mod_1_drop_posts_hidden_by_fk_unbreaks_feed_embed`: dropped the FK, kept `hidden_by` as a plain uuid audit column (verified the live REST embed returns rows again). **LESSON: a 2nd `posts`тЖТ`profiles` FK breaks the bare `profiles(...)` embed тАФ the same trap already documented on `getTeam`.** **Hardened (commit `2d9ae4b5`):** all 7 `posts`тЖТ`profiles` embeds are now qualified to `profiles!posts_author_id_fkey(...)` (6 feed queries in `posts.js` + the trending query in `Discover.js`), verified against live REST тАФ so re-adding a `posts`тЖТ`profiles` FK (incl. `hidden_by`'s, or an `edited_by`) is now safe. `hidden_by` is currently kept as a plain uuid (no FK) тАФ fine for an audit column; re-add the FK only if referential integrity is wanted. **As built:** UI Hide action wired into the tournament + league FeedTabs (`PostActionMenu` `canModerate` from `isDirector`/`isCommissioner`); soft-hide via `set_post_hidden`; `set_comment_hidden` + a new `is_hidden` filter on `getComments` make comment-hiding work backend-side; the RPCs ALSO authorize `is_team_manager` for `team_id` posts, but the **team-feed Hide UI is not yet wired** (TeamFeed still shows Report/Block only) тАФ fast follow. **Fast follow:** surface a comment-Hide menu where tournament/league comments render; a director "Hidden posts" review/unhide list; team-feed Hide UI. NOT pilot-blocking, high pilot-credibility.
- **`FEED-COLDSTART-1` тАФ new users never see a blank feed (тЬЕ FIXED + LIVE, Jun 2; commit `95b550c5`).** **Symptom:** a brand-new account (follows nobody) landed on the default **Following** tab тЖТ empty тЖТ blank wall. **Root cause was the default tab, NOT the query** тАФ contrary to a cold-start spec that assumed "For You" was secretly follow-gated. In the live code `getPosts` (the For You tab) was already global + ungated with the full `avatar_url`/`post_mentions` select; the bug was `Feed.js` `useState('following')` ([Feed.js:407](src/pages/Feed.js:407)). The 28 global seed posts were present + visible the whole time (0 hidden, 0 flagged тАФ verified). **Fix (Option B):** Following stays the default, but when `getFollowingPosts` returns empty we fall back to `getPosts` (global) and show a subtle "тЬи Showing popular chirps тАФ follow players to personalize" hint; `loadMore` tracks the fallback source so pagination stays consistent. No DB change. **Do NOT run** the spec's blanket `DELETE FROM follows тАж` cleanup тАФ it's unscoped and would also remove genuine follows of the 8 seed accounts; the synthetic follows + `tr_auto_follow_seed_accounts` are harmless now that the feed self-heals. **Future:** onboarding "suggested follows" screen (the durable replacement for synthetic follows), then engagement-ranked For You.
- **`ARCH-DUAL-1` тАФ "Dual-empire" architecture: one engine, two skins, one lifetime player (DIRECTION тАФ strategic, Jun 2).** North-star confirmed: serve BOTH youth-competitive (e.g. MHT 10U AAA) and adult-social (BLPA) on ONE unified engine; the UI flips its "skin" by tenant type, the data model **never branches by age.** **(1) Unified schema + a config flag, not a fork.** The abstract chain (Org тЖТ Tournament тЖТ Division тЖТ Team тЖТ Roster тЖТ Game) is identical regardless of age; add a single `feature_profile` value (`youth_competitive` | `adult_social` | тАж) as the one downstream switch. **Verified Jun 2:** `tournaments.settings` + `leagues.settings` JSONB already exist (tiebreakers / format presets live there) тАФ `feature_profile` can ride there **today**, no new table needed. A dedicated `organizations` parent + `organization_settings` is the cleaner long-term home (**NB: no `organizations` table exists yet** тАФ tournaments/leagues are top-level with `director_id`/`commissioner_id`; an org layer would be net-new). **(2) Config-driven UI, never `if (isYouth)` branches.** Read `feature_profile` once at login тЖТ hydrate a feature-flag context (`showAdvancedStats`, `showLockerRoom`, `enforceRosterLocks`, тАж) тЖТ same components, different props; a new tenant type becomes a config row, not a code deploy. Youth dials UP logistics/analytics (roster constraints, box scores, standings); adult dials UP community (team chat, media feed, social). **(3) Global player identity = the moat.** `profiles` is **already** a single global table with no tenant/org FK (verified) тАФ never tenant-scope it, never delete on "age-out." Rosters reference the profile, so the 12-yr-old's youth stats and the 27-yr-old's beer-league team hang off the same identity тЖТ lifetime value LeagueApps structurally can't match (siloed per-org). **This layer IS `IDENT-1`** (the base64-email тЖТ cross-event stat spine; the scaffolded `players` table exists but is empty) тАФ ARCH-DUAL-1 is its strategic frame, build IDENT-1 to realize it. **Caveat тАФ design in now (cheap), retrofit later (expensive):** lifetime history grows forever and never churns out тЖТ plan season-level cold-storage/archival so hot tables stay fast + free-tier-friendly. **The one rule that keeps it one empire not two: youth/adult is a CONFIG VALUE, never a code path.** Not pilot-blocking; informs every multi-tenant decision (pairs with the unified-platform mandate + the multi-division build).
- **`PAD-1` тАФ Rinkd Pad: scorer's-bench hardware (serial scoreboard pass-through + hardware-clock truth + arena audio + LiveBarn scorebug) (DIRECTION тАФ strategic/R&D, phased + funding-gated, Jun 2).** Full spec: `~/Documents/Claude/Projects/Rinkd/Rinkd_Pad_Technical_Spec.md`. **The bet:** a Raspberry-Pi-5 wedge device at the scorer's bench that **pass-throughs the rink's EXISTING scoreboard serial signal** (read-only first, no rink hardware swap), making the **physical board's hardware clock the authoritative game timestamp**, automates arena audio off game events, and (later) overlays a live scorebug on LiveBarn streams. **Why it matters:** this is the unlock for **GS-3** (in-app game clock), which we HELD on purpose тАФ a manual app clock drifts тЖТ confident-but-wrong timestamps. Reading the real board clock makes accurate TOI/PP/per-period stats real, not estimated. Serial-pass-through-to-existing-boards + cloud stats + scorer UI is an unoccupied combo (vs GameSheet/ScoreVision/etc.). **тЪая╕П THE MOAT IS PHASE 3, NOT PHASE 1:** Phase 1 (software-only, "Pad owns the clock") still has a human start/stop a clock тЖТ the SAME drift GS-3 was held for; Phase 1 is a UX/packaging win (two-surface game admin + live game card), NOT the accuracy unlock тАФ don't over-invest in it. **Phases:** P1 software two-device admin (timekeeper screen + scorer phone, shared `game_id`, live sync) тАФ **post-pilot; the only near-term candidate; do NOT touch the Jun 13 pilot (ScorerView works тАФ freeze).** P2 Pi kiosk + audio + PoE/LTE (~4тАУ6 wk). P3 **CTS serial READ = the GS-3-resolving milestone** (Daktronics/Electro-Mech later, reverse-engineer per brand). P4 serial *injection* (control the board) + enclosure + FCC + manufacturing run + LiveBarn + ~$99тАУ199/mo rink lease тАФ **funding/focus-gated.** **Schema reality (checked Jun 2):** `rinks` ALREADY exists with `live_barn_venue_id` + `youtube_url` тЖТ **extend** it (`scoreboard_brand`/`scoreboard_protocol`), don't create; `games.rink_id` exists. The spec's `game_events` table is net-new and **overlaps the existing typed stat tables** (`game_goals`/`game_penalties`/`game_lineups`/`game_shots`) тАФ reconcile to one source of truth, don't just bolt on a parallel model. `game_events.player_id тЖТ players` ties to **IDENT-1** (the scaffolded-but-empty `players` spine тАФ Pad stat value compounds only once IDENT-1 lands). **Risks:** hardware is a focus + capital pivot for a solo pre-seed founder (Pi ops, per-brand serial reverse-engineering, enclosure, FCC, manufacturing, inventory financing, rink support); the pass-through device MUST **fail-open** (relay bypass) so a Pad failure never kills the live board mid-game; injecting commands into a real board mid-event = liability тЖТ Phase 4, earn trust first. **In tension with `SOCIAL-2`** (GameSheet poller = additive wedge, zero hardware, fits the current "run alongside their stack" GTM) тАФ the Pad is an own-the-rink land-grab to fund later; both can coexist. **LiveBarn = a pitch, NOT a partnership** тАФ the hooks (`live_barn_venue_id`) exist, but don't build to their API until they commit. **Patent:** a ~$320 USPTO provisional before any public demo is cheap insurance for the novel claims (serial pass-through + hardware-clock-as-authoritative-timestamp); time-sensitive vs the pilot тАФ Pete decision. **Nothing here ships before Jun 14; not pilot-blocking.**
- **`LEAGUE-DIV-1` тАФ league divisions (+ OTL standings) (тЬЕ SHIPPED + LIVE тАФ M1тАУM4 merged to `main` Jun 2, commit `f193b160`).** Full spec: `rinkd_v4/LEAGUE_DIVISIONS_BUILD.md`. The **league-side equivalent of MULTIDIV-1** (mirrors the staged-view + cutover pattern). **Driver:** Cincinnati Adult Hockey League (CAHL) тАФ 14 divisions under one league, ~1,750 players; each division its own teams/standings/schedule/playoffs. **Model (Pete sign-off Jun 2):** new `league_divisions` table + nullable `division_id` FKs on `league_teams` + `league_games`; backfill every existing league to one **"Main"** division (KOHA/ESHL render byte-identical); staged **`league_standings_md`** view (partition by `(league_id, division_id)`, `security_invoker=on`, read via a `STANDINGS_VIEW` constant); commissioner Divisions tab + an adaptive division selector on both manage + public (both **only when >1 division**); per-division schedules (no crossover v1); per-division playoff brackets. **Division navigation scales by count + is team-anchored (Decision #6, NOT a flat chip row тАФ 14 divisions would be unusable):** logged-in members **land on their own division** (resolved via team membership, reusing the NAV-PIN-1 chain); **chips тЙд5 divisions, a searchable tier-grouped picker >5, nothing for single-division**; Teams tab grouped-by-division + search; `?division=` URL param for shareable/reload-safe scope. **Per-division rules inherit the league for v1** (`league_divisions.settings` plumbed, no UI). **OTL folded in** (Pete's call): live view is W/L/T-only + `league_games` has no OT/SO marker тЖТ adds `decided_in`('regulation'|'ot'|'so') + `shootout_winner` columns + ScorerView capture + an OTL column + config-driven points (`points_otl` default 1) тАФ backward-compatible (existing games backfill `regulation` тЖТ OTL=0 тЖТ standings value/rank-identical). **Required new RLS:** commissioner-gated `league_teams_update` (none exists today тАФ teamтЖТdivision assignment would silently no-op without it). **Milestones:** M1 schema+backfill+staged view (~2тАУ3 d) ┬╖ M2 public division nav (team-anchored default + adaptive picker + `?division=` + grouped Teams) + OTL column (~1.5тАУ2 d) ┬╖ M3 commissioner CRUD + scope selector + OTL capture (~2тАУ3 d) ┬╖ M4 schedule/playoff scoping + **cutover** (~1.5тАУ2 d). **~7.5тАУ10 d.** **Cutover may ship PRE-pilot** (Decision #5 тАФ league_standings is isolated from the BLPA `tournament_standings` path). Build on `feature/league-divisions`. **ЁЯЪз M1 DONE (Jun 2).** **LIVE ON PROD** (additive, pilot-safe тАФ live `league_standings` untouched): migrations `league_divisions_additive_schema_and_backfill` (table + nullable `division_id` FKs on `league_teams`/`league_games` + OTL cols `decided_in`/`shootout_winner` + RLS incl. the **new commissioner-gated `league_teams` UPDATE/DELETE** + backfill one "Main" division/league, **0 unassigned**), `league_standings_md_staged_division_scoped_otl_view` (the staged view тАФ **byte-identical to live: 6=6 rows, both EXCEPT diffs = 0, OTL sum 0**; advisor **0-ERROR**), and `create_league_team_add_division_id_param` (now takes `p_division_id`, validated in-league). Branch code (commits pushed to `feature/league-divisions`, **NOT on main**): `STANDINGS_VIEW='league_standings_md'` constant + `getLeagueStandings(leagueId, divisionId?)` in `src/lib/leagues.js`. **ЁЯЪз M2 DONE (Jun 2)** тАФ public division nav in `League.js`: `selectedDivisionId` resolves `?division=` URL param тЖТ the user's own division (`getMyDivisionInLeague`, team-membership chain) тЖТ first by sort_order; new shared `src/components/DivisionPicker.js` (nothing тЙд1 / chips 2тАУ5 / searchable picker >5 тАФ CAHL's 14); Schedule + Standings scoped to the division; Teams tab is a cross-division finder (grouped + search) when multi; OTL standings column shown only once `otl>0` (so existing leagues are byte-identical until M3 capture); new `src/lib/leagueDivisions.js`. Compiles clean. **ЁЯЪз M3 DONE (Jun 2).** **(part 1)** `LeagueManage`: new **Divisions tab** (add/rename/reorder тЦ▓тЦ╝/delete-with-cascade-warning, blocks deleting the last); **scope picker** on Teams (targets which division new teams join + filters the list); **per-team division dropdown**; new teams (linked + unlinked) land in the selected division. `src/lib/leagueDivisions.js` CRUD (`create/update/delete/reorder/assignLeagueTeamDivision`); `addLeagueTeam` + `create_league_team` carry `division_id`. **(part 2)** `ScorerView` **OT/SO capture** тАФ at league finalize, "How did it end?" (unequal тЖТ Regulation/Overtime; tied тЖТ Tie/Shootout + winner pick, finalize-blocked until picked) writes `league_games.decided_in` + `shootout_winner` (home/away тЖТ the `league_teams` UUID); load maps it back. This is the OTL data source. **Verified on a KEPT 3-division demo:** *"Riverbend Adult Hockey League (Demo)"* (Cincinnati; D1/4B/5C; Pete = commissioner; 12 teams; reg+OT+SO games per division) тАФ the staged `league_standings_md` returns three independent rankings with correct W/L/OTL/PTS (SO/OT winтЖТW, lossтЖТOTL 1pt, reg lossтЖТ0). тЪая╕П The demo is **public on live prod now** but only renders as a proper 3-division page on the **branch preview** / after the M4 cutover тАФ on `main` today League.js reads the live `league_standings` (no division partition, no picker) so it shows 12 teams in one combined ranking with SO games as ties. Harmless (labeled "(Demo)"); set `is_public=false` until merge if you'd rather hide it. **ЁЯЪз M4 DONE + CUTOVER COMPLETE (Jun 2).** `bulkInsertLeagueGames(тАж, divisionId?)` + `addLeagueGame` tag generated/manual games with their division; the Schedule + Playoffs manage tabs got a scope picker and the Smart Generator / Advanced builder / PlayoffsTab / single-game form all generate into the selected division (neither generator deletes existing games тЖТ no cross-division wipe). **Cutover:** migration `league_divisions_m4_cutover_rename_standings_view` dropped the old `league_standings` and **renamed `league_standings_md` тЖТ `league_standings`** (no DB dependents; `security_invoker=on` preserved; division_id + otl columns present); the `STANDINGS_VIEW` constant was flipped to `'league_standings'`; **`feature/league-divisions` merged to `main` (`f193b160`) + pushed.** **LEAGUE-DIV-1 is COMPLETE and LIVE.** Single-division leagues (KOHA/ESHL) render byte-identical (proven in M1); the kept *Riverbend Adult Hockey League (Demo)* (D1/4B/5C) now renders as a real 3-division page on prod. тЪая╕П Remaining verification owed (auth-gated, can't drive logged-out): a logged-in eyeball of the picker / per-division standings + the ScorerView "how did it end?" OT/SO flow on a real game. **Deferred polish (not blocking):** per-division feed/push tagging (event-wide today), per-division rules UI (inherits league), inter-divisional crossover games, league tiebreaker-array parity.
- **Admin god mode** (~2-3 days). `/admin/users` search, edit/delete-any-content Edge Function with service role, `profiles.is_suspended` flag, audit log. NO real impersonation (security risk).
- ~~**DB index audit** (~30 min).~~ **Done May 15 evening** тАФ see ┬з5. FK indexes added, RLS initplan refactor shipped, advisor cleaned up.
- **`EMAILVERIFY-1` тАФ Real email verification** (~0.5тАУ1 day, mostly deliverability setup; Pete, June 1). **Current state:** Supabase "Confirm email" is OFF тАФ `email_confirmed_at` is stamped at the same instant as signup (auto-confirm), so junk like `aa@aa.com` gets in with no inbox check. Intentional for the pilot (removes a funnel step; avoids rink-wifi deliverability pain at a live event). **Post-pilot build:** (1) flip **Auth тЖТ Email тЖТ Confirm email** ON; (2) the real work тАФ wire a production sender (Resend/Postmark/SES) on a `rinkd.com` domain with SPF/DKIM, because default Supabase SMTP is rate-limited + lands in spam; (3) pick the gate тАФ soft (let unverified in but nag/limit) vs hard (block until confirmed); soft is friendlier for a social app; (4) backfill тАФ every existing user was created under auto-confirm, so purge obvious junk first and do NOT flip mid-pilot (a misconfig could lock out legit pilot users on their next session). Test the sender before flipping.
- **RLS multiple-permissive cleanup** (~30 min). 80 advisor WARNs remain тАФ most are 2тАУ3 differently-named policies doing the same thing (e.g. `comments_insert_own` + `"Authenticated users can comment"` + `"Users create their own comments"` are all the same INSERT-with-`author_id`-check). Consolidate to one policy per (table, cmd) pair. Behavior-affecting refactor, so do it deliberately and read each cluster before dropping тАФ some pairs are subtly different.

### Tournament engine тАФ GameSheet parity (post-pilot)

Suggested sprint order per the spec doc: iOS PWA banner тЖТ suspensions тЖТ game clock тЖТ offline mode тЖТ (refs + embed in parallel) тЖТ roster validation. All items below have full file:line/migration specs in the parity doc тАФ pull from there, don't re-spec.

| # | Gap | Priority | Effort | Notes |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| GS-1 | **Offline mode** тАФ SW background-sync queue + IndexedDB so a flaky WiFi rink doesn't drop goals/penalties mid-game | **P0 pre-scale** | 8-12 days | Spec includes 5 phases (prefetch, queue, SW drain, banner, conflict resolution). Currently ┬з12 P2 K hand-waves with "paper backup" тАФ fine for one venue, **required before 2nd tournament partner**. New Edge Function `sync-scorekeeper-queue` (service role). No schema changes. |
| GS-2 | **Suspension management** тАФ game-misconduct/match-penalty flow auto-prompts a `game_suspensions` row; director sees pending suspensions tab; suspended players badged on standings | **P1** | 2-3 days | New `game_suspensions` table. | GS-3 | **In-app game clock** тАФ counts down period length, auto-pre-fills `time_in_period` on goal/penalty save | **тП╕я╕П HELD May 21, 2026** | тАФ | **Not building.** No arena-scoreboard sync exists, so a manual app clock drifts by minutes тЖТ confident-but-wrong timestamps on the official record (worse than an empty field). Revisit only if a venue staffs ONE person for clock+scoresheet. See ┬з5 May 21 entry + memory `feature-judgment-correctness-over-convenience`. |
| GS-4 | **Referee tracking** тАФ assign refs per game, post-tournament ref analytics (penalties called, misconducts) | **P2** | 2-3 days | New `referees` + `game_referees` tables; optional `game_penalties.referee_id` FK. Pre-game ref assignment UI. Per-ref stats from existing penalty joins. **Gemini analysis (May 26) adds two extensions to fold in when built:** (a) **scoresheet signature lock** тАФ official's digital signature locks the game record at final (accountability/safety for youth), a small add; (b) **Demosphere-style assignment logic** тАФ auto-assign refs across a whole schedule, which is the BIZ-3 marketplace layer below. Core assign+analytics stays P2. |

> **GS-2 (suspensions) + GS-5 (roster validation) are subsumed/advanced by the multi-division build below** (jersey-keyed + advisory, no dependency on the gated `players` backfill).

### `TOURN-SCHED-1` тАФ Tournament smart scheduler (target-games + multi-sheet) тАФ SPEC'd Jun 1, 2026 (3v3 driver)
**Why:** the tournament wizard's `generateRoundRobin` (TournamentCreate.js Step 4) is full round-robin only, single-rink, back-to-back from one start time. Fine for an 8-team pool; falls apart for a dense event (esp. **3v3**: many teams, short games, 2тАУ4 sheets running in parallel, guarantee "N games then bracket"). The league side already has the smart half (`src/lib/leagueScheduleGenerator.js`: `computeScheduleShape` target-games + home/away meeting-flip) but it's single-rink and week-oriented. This ports + extends it to tournaments. **The two genuinely new capabilities vs. either existing generator: (1) parallel rinks, (2) rest/back-to-back avoidance.**
**Reuse:** `roundRobinPairs` (tournamentManage.js) for pairings + bye handling; `computeScheduleShape` + the even-meeting home/away flip (lift from leagueScheduleGenerator.js); keep the existing wizard's pool-awareness (per-pool RR) and in-memory team shape (teams have no DB ids at Step 4 тАФ home/away are names).
**New pure module `src/lib/tournamentScheduleGenerator.js`:**
- `generateTournamentSchedule({ teams, targetGamesPerTeam, startDateTime, rinks[], gameBlockMinutes, dayWindow:{startHour,endHour}, minRestMinutes })` тЖТ `{ rows:[{home, away, pool, rink, time}], shape:{meetingsPerPair,gamesPerTeam,totalGames}, warnings[] }`.
- **Per pool:** `computeScheduleShape` so a 16-team pool doesn't force a 15-game RR тАФ it gives the requested ~N (e.g. target 5 тЖТ 1 RR meeting). Build `meetingsPerPair` round-robins, flip home/away on even meetings for balance.
- **Slotting (the new algorithm):** maintain a per-rink time cursor + a per-team `lastEnd` map. Greedily place each pairing into the **earliest rink slot тЙе max(both teams' lastEnd + minRestMinutes)**; advance that rink's cursor by `gameBlockMinutes`, roll to next day at `endHour`тЖТnext day `startHour`. This parallelizes sheets AND spreads each team's games. Deterministic (stable team order) so the live preview is stable.
- **Pure тЖТ live preview:** "48 games ┬╖ 6 per team ┬╖ 2 sheets ┬╖ ends Sat 7:40 PM" recomputed on every form change, no DB.
**Wizard UI (TournamentCreate Step 4):** add a **"Smart fill"** mode next to the existing round-robin button. Inputs: target games/team, multi-select which rinks to use, game-block minutes, daily window (start/end hour), min rest. Preview card + a warnings list. Writes into `data.games` in the existing shape тАФ zero changes to publish/insert path downstream.
**Bracket handoff:** smart fill covers **pool play only**; the bracket stays the separate Generate-Bracket step (`advancement_per_pool` already exists). Optional v2: reserve a bracket time-block after the last pool slot.
**Warnings / edge cases:** odd team count тЖТ `roundRobinPairs` bye (no double-book); single rink selected тЖТ degrades to today's sequential behavior; window too small тЖТ "needs ~X more hours / another sheet"; min-rest infeasible (too few sheets for team count) тЖТ warn + suggest min sheets. Never silently produce a back-to-back.
**Effort ~1тАУ1.5 days:** pure generator + tests ~0.5d (it's the circle method + a greedy slotter), wizard UI + preview ~0.5d, edge-case polish ~0.5d. **Out of scope:** ref/scorekeeper assignment, ice-cost optimization, cross-pool seeding constraints.

(2) **eligibility = advisory + roster freeze** тАФ flag (don't block) no-prelim-game + missing USA Hockey # (self-attested, no API); `game_lineups` already tracks participation. Don't touch the activation gate / scoring RLS beyond threading `division_id`. Also the product side of the per-division pricing add-on already on `/pricing`.

Live preview re-runs the pure generator on every form change (no DB hit). Two-tap confirm before insert. Existing modal-based "Advanced" wizard kept as secondary path.
- тЬЕ `src/pages/LeagueCreate.js` тАФ `FORMAT_PRESETS` expanded from 1 to **4 presets**: `classic_league`, `beer_league_no_ties`, `high_school_style`, `youth_short_game`.
- тЬЕ Build clean (+2.37 kB gz). Advisor 0-ERROR. DB smoke tests pass.

**Phase 3b тАФ тЬЕ SHIPPED** (pending Pete's merge of `claude/laughing-nightingale-10d576`, same branch as Phase 1 + Phase 2 + Phase 3a):
- тЬЕ Migration `league_games_add_round_for_playoff_bracket` тАФ `round text` column + partial composite index `(league_id, phase, round) WHERE phase='playoffs'`.
- тЬЕ New `src/lib/leaguePlayoffGenerator.js` тАФ pure functions: `seedPairs`, `firstRoundLabel`, `generatePlayoffRoundOne`, `generatePlayoffNextRound`. Standard cross-bracket seeding (1v8/4v5/3v6/2v7 etc.); winner-pairing math for round N+1; optional bronze-game checkbox for the post-semis state.
- тЬЕ `src/pages/LeagueManage.js` тАФ new 'Playoffs' tab. Inline `PlayoffsTab` (~270 lines) with bracket size + scheduling form + live preview + standings seeding card + current-bracket display grouped by round.
- тЬЕ Discovered + worked around structural constraint: `league_games.home_team_id`/`away_team_id` are NOT NULL (unlike tournament games), so the generator emits one round at a time with real teams тАФ no TBD placeholders. Commissioner re-runs after each round to seed the next.
- тЬЕ Build clean (+3.5 kB gz). Advisor 0-ERROR. DB smoke pass.

**Phase 3 тАФ тЬЕ COMPLETE.** All four pieces from the original Phase 3 spec shipped (`league_games.phase`, smart scheduler, playoff bracket UI, more presets).

**Deferred polish (post-pilot backlog, not pilot-blocking):**
- Per-rink balancing in the smart scheduler (today: single-rink; commissioners run separately per rink + interleave).
- Smart-schedule batch edit (today: per-game inline edit works fine).
- Phase selector on the manual "Add Single Game" form (today: rare edge case; SQL).
- 6-team bracket with byes (today: 2/4/8 only).
- Bracket auto-fill on game finalize (today: commissioner re-runs the generator after each round finalizes).

Total program effort: Phase 1 ~1 day, Phase 2 ~1 day, Phase 3a ~0.5 day, Phase 3b ~0.5 day тАФ **~3 days actual vs the original 10-14 day estimate.** Done.

### League engine тАФ LeagueApps parity (post-pilot)

Spec'd in **`rinkd_v4/LEAGUEAPPS_PARITY_GAPS.md`** (May 17). 8 gaps for the league-management surface (vs the tournament surface above). Per the spec doc: BLPA Cleveland is tournaments, **none of these are pilot-blocking**. First milestone after Cleveland per the doc: LA-1 (Stripe registration) + LA-2 (Waivers). Everything else is table stakes after that. **Note (May 19):** the tournament-parity build above (`LEAGUE_PARITY_PHASE_1_BUILD.md`) is a separate workstream from these LeagueApps-parity items тАФ the parity build is foundational UX/scheduling, while these LA-* items are commercial features (Stripe, waivers, eligibility). The parity build should ship FIRST since it unblocks the entire league surface.

|---|---|---|---|---|

Crossbar (built-in), SportsEngine (NCSI), PlayMetrics (built-in clearance) all have this тАФ a **deal-breaker** for any sanctioned-youth / school-affiliated partner. **Partner integration (Checkr or NCSI API), NOT in-house.** New `clearance_status` on the coach/volunteer profile + a compliance gate on activation. Same youth/sanctioned-only scope as LA-3; pairs with the coach/volunteer onboarding + household/registration work. **Skip unless Rinkd pursues youth/sanctioned leagues.** |

### ЁЯТ│ Payments & Registration тАФ state of play (May 26, 2026)

Consolidated map after the May 26 payments build, so the next decision is made from one place. Pete **paused** further payments work here pending a direction call.

**тЬЕ LIVE (built + deployed + verified):**
- **Team-level registration + one-time payment** тАФ leagues (`LA-1`) + tournaments (`TOURN-REG-1`). Public `/league/:id/register` + `/tournament/:id/register` pages; commissioner/director **Registrations tab** (open toggle / fee / deadline / max-teams / copy-link, approve┬╖waitlist┬╖reject, CSV export). Free *and* paid. Auto-creates the team row on payment (webhook, idempotent). `stripe-checkout` + `stripe-webhook` are **polymorphic by `kind`**.
- **Stripe Connect (Express) тАФ OPTIONAL** (`BIZ-INFRA-1`). When an organizer connects payouts тЖТ destination charge, **99% to them / 1% to Rinkd**, Stripe processing grossed up to the registrant. When NOT connected тЖТ the fee collects into Rinkd's platform account (settle manually). Enabling Connect needs the org's Stripe ID/KYC + a one-time platform enable тАФ deferred, not blocking.
- **The 1% platform fee** тАФ applies on the Connect/destination-charge path only (no Connect = full amount to Rinkd's account).

**ЁЯУЭ SPEC'D, model signed off (`REGISTRATION_PARITY.md`), NOT built тАФ the big "registration + household + payments" rock (design-first; get Pete sign-off on model+flow before code):**
- **Per-player / participant charging** (vs today's team-level). Needs first-class participants тЖТ households (`REG-2`).
- **Payer/participant portal** тАФ "what you owe / pay / receipts / autopay" (`FAMILY-1`). тЪая╕П today's **"Dues Tracker" is an empty `ComingSoon` placeholder** тАФ this is its intended home.
- **Installments / split payments / payment plans + AR aging** тАФ Crossbar parity (`CROSSBAR-1`).
- **Households / guardians / login-less minors** (`REG-2`).

**ЁЯФЬ NOT built тАФ smaller, independent items:**
- **Subscriptions / recurring** тАФ season dues (recurring) + Crease premium $4.99/mo (`MONEY-1`, consumer track). Different Stripe mode; can coexist but each is its own build. Season-dues recurring should ride the same registrations/payment-plan schema. **Crease premium is now build-ready spec'd тАФ see the `MONEY-1` subsection just below (~80% done; only the Stripe wiring is left).**
- **Native store checkout** тАФ store is **affiliate link-outs + a "Rinkd Merch coming soon" placeholder** today. Native checkout is feasible (reuses the Checkout pattern, no Connect тАФ Rinkd sells its own gear) but needs **fulfillment (Printful) + shipping + tax**. Small, self-contained build.

**Sequencing note:** items 1тАУ4 above are facets of ONE workstream (the unified registration/household/payment-plan system) тАФ multi-week, design-first. The store + Crease subscription are independent smaller builds.

### `MONEY-1` тАФ Crease subscription (build-ready spec, May 27 2026)

**~80% done тАФ the entitlement layer already exists; only the Stripe wiring is missing.** Already built: `crease_subscriptions` (`user_id`, `stripe_subscription_id`, `status` default `'active'`, `current_period_end`, `created/updated_at`); `has_crease_access(p_user_id)` RPC + client `hasCreaseAccess()` (`src/lib/crease.js`); `profiles.is_premium` / `premium_until` / `stripe_customer_id` (manual hand-onboard override, frozen for non-admins by the May 25 guard trigger тАФ service role bypasses); `CreasePaywall.js` (reads `REACT_APP_CREASE_PAYMENTS_LIVE` + `REACT_APP_CREASE_CHECKOUT_URL`, fails safe, fires `crease_paywall_shown` / `crease_subscribe_clicked`); the `stripe-webhook` endpoint itself (verify_jwt=false, signature-verified).

**Approach тАФ Stripe Payment Link, NOT a dynamic checkout fn.** The paywall CTA is already an `<a href>` and the env var is named `..._CHECKOUT_URL` тАФ designed for a static link. A Payment Link gets the 7-day trial, tax, SCA, Apple/Google Pay, and the cancel-anytime Customer Portal with **zero backend code**. Upgrade to a dynamic Checkout fn later (only needed for per-user coupons / in-app trial logic) is non-breaking.

**Build (small):**
1. **Stripe dashboard (testтЖТlive):** product "Crease Premium" тЖТ recurring **$4.99/mo** price (`trial_period_days: 7`) тЖТ **Payment Link** (collect email; enable Customer Portal).
2. **`CreasePaywall.js`:** pass the current `userId` in (from `Crease.js` / `CreaseEpisode.js` / `CreaseShow.js`, or `useAuth()`); append `?client_reference_id=${userId}&prefilled_email=тАж` to the link тАФ the durable map-back (mirrors registration's `metadata.registration_id`).
3. **`stripe-webhook/index.ts`:** add a `session.mode === "subscription"` branch **BEFORE** the existing `kind=league|tournament` registration logic тЪая╕П (today *every* `checkout.session.completed` defaults to a registration; a sub session has no `registration_id` so it currently no-op-acks тАФ harmless, but the short-circuit MUST go first). On that branch: upsert `crease_subscriptions` (`user_id` тЖР `client_reference_id`, `stripe_subscription_id` тЖР `session.subscription`, `status`, `current_period_end`) + stamp `profiles.stripe_customer_id` тЖР `session.customer`. Add `customer.subscription.updated` / `.deleted` handlers тЖТ update `status` + `current_period_end` keyed by `stripe_subscription_id` (service role bypasses RLS + the profiles guard). `invoice.*` optional тАФ `subscription.updated` already carries period + status.
4. **Vercel env** (once Link + webhook live): `REACT_APP_CREASE_CHECKOUT_URL` = the Link; `REACT_APP_CREASE_PAYMENTS_LIVE` = `1`.

**Pete's dashboard steps (mirror LA-1):** create the product + price + Payment Link; add **`customer.subscription.created` / `.updated` / `.deleted`** to the existing `stripe-webhook` endpoint's subscribed events (`checkout.session.completed` is already subscribed).

**Open decisions:** keep the 7-day trial? ┬╖ v1 cancel/manage = Stripe's no-code Customer Portal link in Settings (in-app "Manage subscription" button = a small `create-portal-session` fn later) ┬╖ optional `cancel_at_period_end` boolean on `crease_subscriptions` for a "renews/ends on X" UI ┬╖ тЪая╕П **content hardening (separate, not v1-blocking):** the gate is *soft* (client/RPC decide whether to render) тАФ if episode media URLs are public, a determined user can fetch them directly; true protection = signed URLs from an edge fn that calls `has_crease_access()`.

**No MCP Write needed** тАФ the Payment Link creates the product+price inline. To scaffold the test product/price programmatically instead, grant Write (products/prices, test mode) via `/mcp`.

### тнР Registration & unified-platform design mandate (Pete, May 23 тАФ READ BEFORE building any registration/payment/household work)

**тЖТ DESIGN DOC (May 25): [`rinkd_v4/REGISTRATION_PARITY.md`](../rinkd_v4/REGISTRATION_PARITY.md) тАФ the model is signed off (4 forks). This section + the IA seed below are the rationale; the doc is the spec. ┬з6 of the doc lists the remaining open questions for a final pre-build pass.**

**This is the hard part, and it's the whole bet. Treat it accordingly.** The thesis: every competitor makes you stitch together a scoring tool + a registration tool + a payments tool + a comms tool. Rinkd's bet is **everything in one social-media-style app** тАФ and the *only* reason that's defensible is if it stays **intuitive, simple, and easy for literally anyone** (a hockey parent, a beer-league captain, a volunteer commissioner). **Pete's read on why no one has unified this before: because the moment you combine registration + payments + households + scheduling + scoring + social, it gets messy and chaotic тАФ so the deliberate, clean design IS the moat.** If it's confusing, we've built nothing better than the incumbents.

**Approach this like a product/eng lead at Google / Amazon / Facebook. The architecture and the flow have to be perfect тАФ not "good enough."** Concretely, that means:
- **Data model + information architecture FIRST, UI second.** Households, guardians, minor-participants-without-logins, roles (parent vs player vs captain vs commissioner vs director), registrations, payment plans, invoices тАФ get the entities and relationships right before a single screen is drawn. Retrofitting households/installments onto a flat schema is how it becomes chaotic.
- **One mental model, ruthless progressive disclosure.** A user only ever sees what's relevant to their role and their context. Hide complexity behind clean defaults; never make a parent reason about the commissioner's view or vice versa.
- **Make it feel native to the social app, not bolted-on.** Reuse the patterns that already work (feed, follow, notifications, the existing role-gating) so "register my kid" and "pay my invoice" feel like the same product as "chirp" and "follow my team," not a separate portal grafted on.
- **Every flow must be self-evident on a phone, first try, no manual.** If a step needs explaining, redesign the step.
- **Design the schema once, surface it from every side.** Org-admin money view (Crossbar), family payment view (LeagueApps), player/parent self-service тАФ all the same underlying `registrations`/payment-plan data, never duplicated.

When this workstream is picked up: start with a written IA + data-model design (the `rinkd_v4/CROSSBAR_PARITY_GAPS.md` / `REGISTRATION_PARITY.md` doc), get Pete's sign-off on the *flow and model* before building, and hold the bar at "a first-time user gets it instantly." See memory `unified-platform-design-mandate`.

### Household & registration тАФ IA seed (first design pass, May 23, 2026)

The mandate above says "write the IA + data-model before building." **This is the seed** тАФ flesh it into the `REGISTRATION_PARITY.md` doc when scoped. Distilled from a SportsEngine / LeagueApps / Crossbar walkthrough (Pete's own SportsEngine account; screenshots in this session's transcript).

**The core inversion (the moat, made concrete):** every incumbent is a *stack of separate destinations* тАФ Home, Household, Schedule, Teams, Bills, Registrations, Memberships, Credentials, Video (SportsEngine's 11-item nav). That portal/admin model is why they feel heavy. Rinkd inverts it:
- **The Feed IS home.** No separate dashboard. The living stream of chirps + recaps from the people/teams you follow is the landing surface. **Never** greet a user with empty "Nothing scheduled / No teams / No payments" cards (SportsEngine's dead first impression) тАФ for new users, Home onboards (follow your team, here's what's happening).
- **Identity is a switcher, not a console.** "Acting as me / Henry / Audrey" via an avatar switcher (Instagram/Netflix "who's watching" pattern), not a Household page you navigate to. The household is plumbing.
- **Money + registrations are woven in, not destinations.** Collapse Bills + Registrations + Memberships into one per-person money/registration view; surface "you owe $X, due Friday" as a gentle up-next item atop the feed (the one genuinely useful widget on SportsEngine's home). Credentials/eligibility docs (USAH#, SafeSport) surface only when a registration needs one тАФ never standing nav.
- **One person = one card that's everything.** Tap Henry тЖТ his teams, schedule, balance, registration status, docs тАФ one role-scoped screen in the social-app design language.

**Data-model spine:** extend `profiles` (don't invent a parallel "family" system). Add a `guardianships` / household relationship (`guardian_profile тЖТ managed/linked_profile`, role: `owner` / `co_guardian` / `adult_member`). Generalizes the existing [[cshl-personal-tracker]] pattern (Henry #17 = login-less profile via `invite_name`) into a first-class household. The same `registrations` + payment-plan schema is surfaced from every side (org-admin = Crossbar money dashboard, family = LeagueApps payment portal, player self-service) тАФ designed once, never duplicated.

**v1 decisions (Pete, May 23):**
- **Under-13 = no login.** Minors are managed profiles the guardian operates on their behalf (cleanest COPPA posture). Teen/independent access is a later, deliberate add тАФ not v1.
- **Co-parent = shared household.** Multiple adults manage the same kids + see the same bills/schedule (families expect it; retrofitting later is a painful migration).

**Consent / anti-fraud тАФ REQUIRED (Pete: "so people don't just sign up for other people's kids"):** linking to a person is **never unilateral**.
- **Adult тЖФ adult (add a co-guardian, e.g. Audrey):** invite-by-email тЖТ invited adult must **accept**. Mutual consent. Reuse the existing `team_manager_invites` magic-link pattern.
- **Adult тЖТ minor (claim/manage a kid):** creator becomes the kid's **owning guardian**. Any *additional* guardian link, or claiming an existing kid, requires approval from **(a) an existing guardian, OR (b) the org admin (team manager / league commissioner) who rosters the child** тАФ a human vouch. Existing guardians are **notified** on any claim attempt; nothing takes effect until approved.
- **Duplicate guard:** creating a kid that matches an existing rostered minor (name + DOB) in that team/org routes to a **claim request**, not a silent duplicate (handles divorced-parents-both-add-Henry).
- **Org roster is the anchor of truth:** a kid only attaches to teams/registrations when a real team admin rosters them (human-in-the-loop) тАФ a fabricated child can't insert itself onto a team.
- **Audit + escalation:** every guardianship link is audit-logged (who added whom, who approved, when) and reversible; custody disputes escalate to the org admin / Rinkd support тАФ **software never adjudicates custody**.

**What to cut vs the incumbents:** the 11-item left nav. Rinkd keeps the feed + a switcher + per-person cards; payments/registrations/docs are woven in or one tap away. Bar: "a first-time parent registers a kid and pays, on a phone, first try, no manual."

### Crossbar parity тАФ registration + financial tools (post-pilot; tie-in with Stripe/registrations)

**Captured May 23, 2026 (Pete).** Crossbar (crossbarapp.com) is a youth-sports club/league management platform тАФ a third named parity target alongside GameSheet (tournament side) and LeagueApps (league side). **Pete's directive: when we tie in registrations, get parity with Crossbar's league + tournament tools AND specifically their registration/financial tools.** Their registration money surface is the bar to clear.

**What their "Powerful Financial Tools" screen shows (the spec to hit):**
- **Three at-a-glance cash tiles:** Today / Yesterday / Past Due (e.g. $26,250 / $44,755 / $12,510) тАФ daily collected + outstanding AR at a glance.
- **Revenue-by-month bar chart, stacked Paid (green) / Pending (gray) / Past Due (red)**, spanning past *actuals* AND future *projected* months (the pending bars run forward to 1/2023) тАФ i.e. a forward revenue + accounts-receivable view, not just historical.
- **Feature bullets:** "Full control over current registrations" ┬╖ "Ability to modify payment plans" ┬╖ "Detailed reporting, giving you easy access to financial information."

**How this maps to / extends the existing roadmap:** this is the commercial layer that sits on **LA-1 (Stripe registration + payments)** + **TOURN-REG-1** (the shared polymorphic `registrations` build) + **LA-4 (financial reporting)** + **BIZ-INFRA-1 (Stripe Connect)** in the Revenue section below. Crossbar adds three things beyond what LA-4 currently scopes (which was just total collected / outstanding / refunds / Stripe net):
1. **Payment-plan engine** тАФ installment schedules per registration, and the ability to *modify* a plan after the fact (the hard part: proration, re-amortization, dunning on a missed installment).
2. **Projected/pending revenue + AR aging** тАФ "Pending" (scheduled future installments) and "Past Due" (missed) as first-class states, charted forward, with the daily cash tiles.
3. **Registration management surface** тАФ full edit/refund/transfer control over active registrations.

**Action when registrations get scoped:** do a proper Crossbar walkthrough and write **`rinkd_v4/CROSSBAR_PARITY_GAPS.md`** (mirror the GameSheet/LeagueApps gap docs) before building, so LA-1/LA-4/TOURN-REG-1 are designed with the payment-plan + AR-aging + financial-dashboard requirements baked in from the start (retrofitting installments/projections onto a flat one-time-charge schema is painful). Not pilot-relevant; gated on Stripe. (Screenshot lives in this session's transcript.)

### LeagueApps parity тАФ family account + participant payment portal (post-pilot; the matched pair to Crossbar)

**Captured May 23, 2026 (Pete).** Crossbar above = the **organizer's** money dashboard (AR/revenue). This LeagueApps screen = the **family/participant's** self-service side тАФ the other half of the registration story. **Pete's directive (paraphrase): doesn't need to be exactly the same, but users need (1) a way to track their own payments, and (2) a way to manage multiple kids / teams if they have them.** Those two are the keepers; the rest is reference.

**Two essentials (build these):**
1. **Household / family account model** тАФ one parent/guardian account with multiple **child participants** under it ("My Family": guardian + kids; "+ Add Parent/guardian"). Each participant has their own registered activities, schedule, and invoices, all rolled up under the one login. **This is net-new to Rinkd's data model** тАФ today an account is a single flat user. Needs a guardianтЖФparticipant (household) relationship, and participants who may have **no login of their own** (minors тАФ COPPA). This generalizes the existing [[cshl-personal-tracker]] pattern (Henry #17 tracked via `invite_name`, no account) into a real first-class household model. Touches auth/profile architecture тАФ scope it deliberately, not as a bolt-on.
2. **Participant payment portal** тАФ the self-service money view: **Invoices** with Unpaid + Receipts tabs, per-invoice "You owe $X out of $Y", status (e.g. "Payment Plan On Schedule"), view-details + receipts, and **Pay Multiple Invoices**. Plus **Payment Settings**: Auto Pay on/off + stored card + autopay agreements tied to payment plans. This is the participant-facing read of the same `registrations`/payment-plan engine that powers the Crossbar org dashboard тАФ **build the schema once, surface it from both sides** (org admin = Crossbar view, family = this view).

**Reference (don't need parity, captured for the eventual gap doc):** per-participant activity tables (Role/Team ┬╖ Program ┬╖ Payment Paid/Owe ┬╖ Status incl. "Spot Reserved"/"Awaiting Response" ┬╖ Actions = Accept/Decline team invites); a **My Schedule** that merges all family members' schedules labeled by participant; Profiles (family account, per-member profile edit); Settings (password/email prefs, text/comms, mobile-app access for child participants).

**Fold into the same workstream as Crossbar + LA-1/LA-6:** the household model overlaps **LA-6 (multi-season)** conceptually and depends on the **LA-1/TOURN-REG-1 registrations + payment-plan** schema. When scoped, add the family-portal + household requirements to `rinkd_v4/CROSSBAR_PARITY_GAPS.md` (or a sibling `REGISTRATION_PARITY.md`) so the registrations schema is designed for guardians/minors/multi-participant from day one. Post-pilot; gated on Stripe. (Screenshots in this session's transcript.)

### KOHA stats parity (hockeypage replacement) тАФ prioritized May 22, 2026

KOHA's implicit first ask: don't make them lose stats vs their old system (hockeypage.com). Pete sent 8 season exports (standings, scoring, goalies, scoring-by-division, penalty frequency, raw penalty log, playoff scoring + goalies тАФ analyzed this session). **Verdict: full parity is achievable with little-to-no schema change тАФ Rinkd already CAPTURES everything; the gaps are reporting surfaces.** Captured today: `game_goals` (scorer + `assist1_number` + `assist2_number`), `game_penalties` (`penalty_type` + duration + period), `game_shots`, `game_goalie_changes`, `league_games.phase` (reg vs playoff).

**Key design rule: within-season leaderboards aggregate by `(team, jersey#)`, names from `team_members.invite_name` тАФ the Phase-1 Stats tab must NOT depend on accounts (most players have none).** тЪая╕П **But jersey# is a WITHIN-season key only.** KOHA re-drafts every year тАФ new teams, new numbers тАФ so jersey# does NOT carry a player's stats across seasons. **Cross-season / career stats require a persistent identity = the Rinkd account (Phase 2), AND multi-season support (LA-6, not built) to span league-seasons.** Today each KOHA season is effectively its own `league` row, so per-season scoping falls out naturally; jersey# is fine inside one season, useless across them. (`get_player_league_stats` is per-USER тАФ that's the Phase-2 / career path, not the Phase-1 leaderboard.)

**Phasing (Pete, May 22):**
- **Phase 1 тАФ review-only Stats tab. тЬЕ SHIPPED May 23, 2026** (`a2c7a9e3` league, `3e1b57d2` tournament). Jersey-based skater (G/A/PTS/PIM/Pt-G) + goalie (GP/W-L-T/GA/SA/SV%/GAA/SO) leaderboards on both the League and Tournament pages, via `get_league_*` / `get_tournament_*` stat RPCs + shared `StatLeaderboards.js`. No accounts needed for players to appear (names from `team_members` for leagues, `game_lineups` for tournaments). See the ┬з5 "May 23 тАФ Stat leaderboards" entry for the full data-model + validation detail. **Two corrections to the original plan:** (a) the Stats tab is **login-gated**, NOT anon-public тАФ live data (standings/schedule/stats) requires sign-in on both surfaces by deliberate decision (Pete, May 23: maximize sign-ups). KOHA reviewing "via a shared link" therefore means *signed-in* viewers; exposing stats on the public landing is a future Pete call only. (b) The league **goalie board is per-TEAM goaltending**, not per-goalie тАФ league scoring doesn't capture goalie-in-net, so it's attributed to the lone roster goalie when a team has one (per-goalie league stats need a scoring-flow change; see follow-ups).
- **Phase 2 тАФ tie to profiles.** Once players sign up + link to their roster row (`link_invited_player` backfills `user_id`), the same jersey-keyed stats surface on player profiles. No rebuild тАФ accounts attach on top of the jersey aggregation. (The Phase-1 RPCs already fall back to `profiles.name` when `team_members.user_id` is set.) **STATUS (May 26):** the LEAGUE side is **already live** тАФ `Profile.js` Stats tab calls `get_player_league_stats(p_user_id)`, which returns **one row per (league ┬╖ season ┬╖ team)** broken out under a "Season Totals ┬╖ across N leagues" header. **Tournament stats are NOT on the profile at all** (no `get_player_tournament_stats`).

  **тнР DECISION (Pete, May 26) тАФ player-profile stats keep league + tournament SEPARATED; never one blended line.** They aren't comparable (a 30тАУ40-game season vs a 3тАУ4-game weekend; different competition levels per event; tournament stats are also per-division). The profile should have two clearly-labeled sections тАФ **"Leagues"** (per league-season, as today) and **"Tournaments"** (per event) тАФ and the cross-context "Season Totals" rollup stays **league-only** (or gets relabeled), never absorbing tournament games. **Build:** add a `get_player_tournament_stats(p_user_id)` RPC mirroring `get_player_league_stats` (keyed on tournament `game_lineups` + `game_goals`/`game_penalties`, returning per-tournament rows incl. division). Tracked as **STATS-3**. Caveats: jersey# is a within-season key (cross-season/career needs the account link + LA-6 multi-season); `get_top_scorers` (global) is still GATE-2 (empty/gated).

**Parity gap list тАФ remaining after Phase 1 (reporting surfaces; ~no schema change unless noted):**
1. ~~**Goalie leaderboard (GAA/SV%)**~~ тЬЕ done Phase 1 (per-team for leagues, per-goalie for tournaments). True **per-goalie league** GAA/SV% needs capturing goalie-in-net during league scoring (schema/flow change) тАФ now tracked as **`GOALIE-1`** (Jun 4): the scorer picks **which goalie was in net** (per goal/period + goalie changes via existing `game_goalie_changes`), and **rosters can carry multiple goalies**. Unblocks per-goalie league boards **and goalie *sub* stats** (`SUBS-1` spec ┬з9.2, which otherwise ships the goalie pool as roster+comms only). ~3-5 d.
2. **Penalty frequency-by-type + raw-penalty export** тАФ aggregation of `game_penalties` (overlaps LA-7). Phase-1 ships team PIM (standings) + player PIM (skater board); the by-type breakdown + export is still TODO.
3. **Phase-split (reg vs playoff) + division-split** on the leaderboards тАФ Phase-1 aggregates all games combined; splitting is TODO. (Team PIM is on the skater board now; adding to `league_standings` view still open.)
4. **Verify `get_top_scorers`** is jersey-based + includes A/PIM тАФ superseded by the new `get_league_skater_stats` RPC for the leaderboard; `get_top_scorers` (per-limit, used elsewhere) left as-is.

Overlaps + extends **LA-7** (commissioner analytics). Phase 1 is live; the remaining items are post-pilot, KOHA-driven.

### Team engine тАФ coaching tools (post-pilot)

Pete's ask (May 17): "line combos and shift tracking, manager/coach runs from the team page." Phased so each piece is shippable on its own; later phases stack onto earlier ones without rework. All work lives on `/team/:id` (existing `Team.js` + `TeamManage.js`) and is coach/manager-gated via the existing `teams.manager_id` check. None of these are pilot-blocking тАФ independent track of work that helps Rinkd compete with TeamSnap / Hockey Coach Vision / SportlyzerCoach for serious/youth/junior teams (BLPA-style rec teams probably won't engage with shift tracking as deeply).

**ROLE-COACH-1 тАФ `coach` is now a first-class team permission (interim = manager-equivalent; shipped May 26, 2026).** Before today, `coach` was only a `team_members.role` display label + a profile position тАФ it carried **zero permissions** (team authority was manager-only). Per Pete, coaches now get **the same permissions as managers for now**: migration `coach_team_perms_and_close_self_insert_escalation` broadened `is_team_manager()` to `role in ('manager','coach')` (one change тЖТ RLS on teams / team_members / team_join_requests / volunteer_slots; `team_games` INSERT already allowed coach), and `Team.js` `isManager` includes coach (тЪЩя╕П Manage + Set Lineup + volunteer-add). The same migration **closed a pre-existing self-insert privilege-escalation** (see the May 26 changelog entry at the top of this doc). **Standing rule (Pete, May 26): as new team-scoped features ship тАФ TEAM-1тАУ4, GS-8 post-game recipients, LA-10 clearances, lineup tools тАФ wire the `coach` role into the gate; treat coach == manager until a distinct coach tier exists. Don't silently leave new features manager-only.** **Future (the roadmap part):** split `coach` into its own **narrower** permission tier once the bench toolkit justifies it тАФ long-term a coach probably shouldn't add/remove *other* managers or delete the team, even if they run lineups/lines/shifts. Until that tier is designed, coach == manager.

| # | Item | Priority | Effort | Notes |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| TEAM-1 | **Line combinations builder** тАФ coach defines forward lines (LW-C-RW ├Ч 4), defense pairs (LD-RD ├Ч 3), goalie rotation. Drag-and-drop from the roster. Multiple saved lineup cards per team (e.g. "Powerplay", "Penalty Kill", "Even Strength"). Visible read-only to roster; editable by manager only. | P2 | 2-3 days | New `team_lineups` table (one row per saved lineup card) + `team_lineup_slots` (player_id ├Ч position ├Ч line_number). New "Lines" tab on `Team.js`. Drag-and-drop UI using HTML5 drag events (no library). Selectable in the existing pre-game lineup flow (extends `game_lineups`). |
| TEAM-2 | **Live shift tracking** тАФ bench-side UI for toggling lines on/off ice during a game. Real-time TOI calculation. Coach taps "Line 1 ON" тЖТ starts a shift timer; taps "Line 2 ON" тЖТ ends Line 1's shift, starts Line 2's. Per-player TOI accumulates from line shifts (no per-player toggle тАФ would be too fiddly on the bench). | P2 | 3-5 days | New `game_shifts` table: `(game_id, lineup_id, line_number, started_at, ended_at, period)`. Requires TEAM-2 to be in place (no shifts = nothing to join against). |

**Suggested order:** TEAM-1 alone is useful for any team with set lines (delivers value at Sprint 1). TEAM-2 unlocks every later phase but is the heaviest UI/UX lift. TEAM-3 + TEAM-4 are stat-nerd features for the most engaged coaches тАФ defer until at least one team is actively using TEAM-2 in live games so the dataset has something to aggregate.

**PlayMetrics parity тАФ tryouts / evaluations / curriculum (future, P3 тАФ Gemini competitive analysis, May 26).** A distinct category from TEAM-1тАУ4 (which are lines/shifts): mobile coach evaluation during tryouts, a drill/curriculum library, session planning, player-development pathways. Premier youth clubs + AAA programs specifically run PlayMetrics for this тАФ it's the long-term moat if Rinkd goes **upmarket** from beer/rec leagues. Phase-2+ product category, not near-term; spin up a `PLAYMETRICS_PARITY_GAPS.md` spec only when that upmarket move is on the table.

### Automated stat content + shareable graphics тАФ growth lever (Gemini, May 26)

**Source:** Gemini competitive analysis (May 26) тАФ a strategic recommendation, not a competitor feature. Turn the stats Rinkd already captures into content shared *outside* the app: auto-generated "Player of the Game" cards, "Top 5 Goalies This Week", "Unbeaten Streak Watch" headlines тАФ branded, cron-generated from box scores + standings. Every share is a free ad at zero marginal cost (the organic-growth loop in the marketing angles, ┬з2 of the analysis doc).

**What exists:** the leaderboard RPCs + `StatLeaderboards.js` (shipped May 23) already aggregate the data; the recap-post flow (`createGameRecapPost`) already drops auto-posts into the feed. **The gap:** a branded visual-card / OG-image generator + a cron that inserts programmatic `rinkside_articles` / feed posts from weekly stat aggregates.

**Priority:** P2 growth lever (~2-3 days). This is the **build half of the Writer-Sourcing "Tier 5: Automated Data News"** GTM playbook (see `Gemini_Competitive_Analysis_Extracts.md` ┬з3) тАФ ship the card generator once and the no-writers-required content stream follows. Overlaps GS-8 (post-game distribution) and the OG-image work.

### Revenue + monetization (post-pilot тАФ Phase 1 + Phase 2)

Spec'd by Pete May 17 + **pricing model locked May 20 via `docs/Rinkd_Pricing_Guide.docx`** (per-size ladder; superseded the old BIZ-TIER-1 4-arrangement model тАФ see the May 20 ┬з5 entry above). Two phases: Phase 1 (0-6 months тАФ Ship Now) and Phase 2 (6-18 months тАФ Build After Cleveland). All revenue items share a foundational dependency on BIZ-INFRA-1 (Stripe Connect platform-fee setup). **Tier enforcement (BIZ-TIER-2) is intentionally post-pilot тАФ don't introduce pricing during Cleveland, ship as Sprint 1 work after.**

> **Pricing-page flow gap (flagged May 21, `73fea303`):** the live `/pricing` page's "Run your league" / "Host your tournament" CTAs currently drop into the **free** create wizard (no payment step) тАФ today's create-free-then-manual-activate model. When this revenue cluster ships (BIZ-INFRA-1 + TOURN-REG-1 + LA-1), route the pricing CTAs into **checkout first** rather than the bare wizard, and retire the manual out-of-band activation for self-serve paid events. See the ┬з5 May 21 entry + memory `pricing-flow-needs-payment-gating`.

**Key pricing decisions captured May 17 (don't re-litigate without explicit Pete review):**
- **Stripe fee absorption:** organizer eats the 2.9% + 30┬в processing fees on every checkout. Standard marketplace practice. Means BLPA gets ~$2,427 of a $2,500 entry fee per team (with $15 BenchBoss + $58 platform fee + Stripe deducted from the $2,515 gross).
- **BenchBoss fee label:** "Technology fee" (not "BenchBoss fee", not "Convenience fee") тАФ softer than naming Rinkd directly, more transparent than vague convenience-fee framing. Standard label teams have seen elsewhere (Ticketmaster-style).
- **Refund policy:** sliding scale тАФ 100% refund >14 days before event, 50% refund 7-14 days out, 0% refund inside 7 days. Technology fee non-refundable once event runs. Industry standard for amateur sports; protects bracket integrity against late dropouts.
- **Crease premium positioning:** kept as a **separate consumer track** (does NOT fold into B2B BenchBoss). Different audience (players + fans), scales independently. MONEY-1 Crease premium remains its own revenue stream alongside BenchBoss/marketplaces; not bundled.

**Phase 1 тАФ Ship Now (0-6 months)**
