#### Entitlements + usage tracking (design тАФ build alongside BIZ-INFRA-1 / TOURN-REG-1 / BIZ-TIER-2)

How we track which package an org bought, the "free tournament with a league plan" cross-sell (so nobody gets a *second* free one), and tier/cap usage once Stripe is live. **`is_activated` stays the RLS gate тАФ it just becomes the OUTPUT of this ledger instead of a manual flip.** Designed May 22 with Pete.

**Three tables:**
- **`purchases`** тАФ immutable record of every Stripe payment (source of truth, written by the webhook): buyer `profile_id`, kind (`league_season` | `tournament_event`), tier, amount, `stripe_payment_intent`/checkout_session, parent (league/tournament id), season, created_at. Only ever mutated to mark refunds.
- **`plans`** тАФ the active grant per league/tournament: owner, parent_type+parent_id, **tier**, **team_cap**, **season**, status (active/expired/refunded), period_start/end, `source_purchase_id`. Drives `is_activated` + the BIZ-TIER-2 team-cap enforcement.
- **`entitlement_credits`** тАФ cross-sell freebies + redemption: owner, type (`free_tournament`), `granted_at`, `expires_at`, **`redeemed_at`** (null until used), `redeemed_on` (tournament id). The "no extra free" guarantee.

**Free-tournament flow:** buy a league season тЖТ webhook writes `purchases` + `plans` (league active) + grants **one** `entitlement_credits` row. Creating/activating a tournament checks for an unredeemed, unexpired credit the buyer owns тЖТ activate free + stamp `redeemed_at`/`redeemed_on`; else normal paid checkout. A second free tournament is structurally impossible without another qualifying league purchase (redemption flips a single row тАФ not a counter that can be gamed).

**Answers the questions:** *what did they order?* тЖТ `plans.tier`/`team_cap`/`season` traced to `purchases`; *free tournament used?* тЖТ `entitlement_credits.redeemed_at`; *over team cap?* тЖТ team count vs `plans.team_cap`; *Year-2 15% off?* тЖТ checkout-time eligibility (active league plan?) тЖТ Stripe coupon (an eligibility lookup, not stored usage).

**Two correctness must-dos:**
1. **Webhook idempotency** тАФ process each Stripe event id exactly once (`processed_stripe_events` table / unique constraint on payment_intent). A re-delivered "payment succeeded" would otherwise double-grant the free credit тАФ the #1 "they got more free" bug.
2. **Activation is derived, not manual** тАФ the webhook + credit redemption set `is_activated`; a refund flips it back + expires the plan. Keep the existing RLS gate; just stop flipping it by hand.

**Open decisions (lock before building):**
1. Free tournament **per league plan** or **per customer per year**? (Org runs 2 leagues = 2 free tournaments, or 1?) тАФ drives per-plan vs per-customer credit granting.
2. **Season boundary** тАФ does a season plan auto-expire on a date, or stay active until the season is marked complete? (affects renewals + when Year-2 pricing kicks in).
3. **Credit expiry** тАФ does an unused free tournament expire at season/year end, or carry forever?

### Still gated on populating `players`
- The canonical `game_events` table backfill.
- Audit High #12's real leaderboard (`get_top_scorers` RPC is correct but returns nothing because `game_lineups` is empty and imported league goals belong to ghost-roster players with no accounts).
- Both unblock once **ChillerStats import + jersey-number тЖТ player_id resolver** runs (needs Pete's machine for internet egress).

### Monetization (gated on user volume)
- Crease premium ($4.99/mo) тАФ UI shipped; **Stripe wiring is now build-ready spec'd (May 27) тЖТ see the `MONEY-1` subsection in the ┬з7 payments map above** (entitlement layer already exists; ~80% done). **Confirmed May 17:** stays as a separate consumer revenue track alongside the B2B BenchBoss/marketplaces. Not bundled.
- ~~BenchBoss/Captain Tier ($15/mo)~~ тАФ **superseded May 17 evening.** The captain-subscription consumer framing in `rinkd_v4/Rinkd_BenchBoss_Captain_Tier_Spec.md` was replaced by the **B2B 4-arrangement BenchBoss billing model** (Community free / Organizer-pays $25/team / Pass-through $15/team Technology fee to participants / Pro custom annual) tracked as **BIZ-TIER-1** in the Revenue + monetization section above. Old spec doc retained as historical reference.

### `ENRICH-1` + `ONBOARD-1` тАФ User profile enrichment + signup streamline (тЬЕ SHIPPED May 28, 2026 тАФ `fbe96c2b`)

**Why:** Rinkd can't segment users by persona / age / gender today and has no first-class dormancy signal тАФ retention campaigns, marketing buckets, and personalization are all impossible. This pass adds the data foundation **and** strips the signup wizard to the bare minimum at the gate so the rest fills in progressively.

**Pete decisions (May 28, sign-off):**
1. **Progressive onboarding** тАФ soft nudge, **no full-screen wall** (aligns with REG-2 ┬з3 "Feed IS home, never empty cards" + the unified-platform mandate).
2. **`date_of_birth date`** тАФ full DOB, not year-only (REG-2 ┬з4.1 alignment; USAH-eligibility-ready; precise under-13 cut).
3. **Adult-only scope** тАФ this spec governs `auth.users` self-signup only. **The login-less under-13 minor `profiles` row + `auth_user_id` decouple + households + consent/audit (REG-2 ┬з4.1/4.3) is untouched and ships later as REG-2 Phase 1.**
4. **Split email opt-in** тАФ separate `transactional` (default TRUE) from `marketing` (default FALSE, opt-in checkbox at signup).

**Relationship to REG-2 (`rinkd_v4/REGISTRATION_PARITY.md`):** the columns added here are **orthogonal** to REG-2's `auth_user_id` / `account_type` / `households` / `household_members` / consent additions тАФ they coexist. Under-13 are hard-blocked from `auth.users` self-signup here; their first-class minor `profiles` rows are created later via REG-2's household-claim flow. **Naming:** the new persona column is **`persona`**, NOT `role`, to avoid collision with `team_members.role` / `tournament_roles.role` / `league_roles.role`.

**Migration: `user_profile_enrichment` (single ALTER TABLE)**
```sql
ALTER TABLE profiles
  ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS date_of_birth date NULL,
  ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS persona text
    CHECK (persona IN ('player','parent','coach','commissioner','official','fan')) DEFAULT NULL,
  ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS gender text
    CHECK (gender IN ('man','woman','non-binary','prefer_not_to_say')) DEFAULT NULL,
  ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS home_rink_id uuid REFERENCES rinks(id) ON DELETE SET NULL,
  ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS last_seen_at timestamptz NULL,
  ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS notification_email_transactional boolean DEFAULT TRUE,
  ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS notification_email_marketing boolean DEFAULT FALSE,
  ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS notification_push boolean DEFAULT TRUE,
  ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS profile_complete boolean DEFAULT FALSE;
```
- **`position` already exists on `profiles`** (Forward/Defense/Goalie). Reuse it тАФ don't duplicate. The signup form writes **`persona`** (player/parent/coach/commissioner/official/fan) AND `position` (Forward/Defense/Goalie; only shown when `persona = 'player'`). Two columns, two constraint sets.
- **`profile_complete`** is the gate for showing the soft-prompt nudge. Flipped TRUE once persona + (position if player) + level are set. App-level decision, not a DB invariant.
- **Extend `profiles_guard_privileged` (May 25 trigger)** to also lock `date_of_birth` after first set тАФ anti-age-fraud (prevents bumping DOB to bypass minor restrictions in marketing). Persona/gender/etc. stay user-editable.

**`get_user_email(p_user_id)` тАФ GATED SECURITY DEFINER (do NOT ship the ungated version):**
```sql
CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION get_user_email(p_user_id uuid)
RETURNS text LANGUAGE sql SECURITY DEFINER SET search_path = public, auth STABLE AS $$
  SELECT u.email FROM auth.users u
  WHERE u.id = p_user_id
    AND (p_user_id = auth.uid()
         OR EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM profiles WHERE id = auth.uid() AND is_admin));
$$;
REVOKE EXECUTE ON FUNCTION get_user_email(uuid) FROM PUBLIC, anon, authenticated;
GRANT  EXECUTE ON FUNCTION get_user_email(uuid) TO authenticated;
```
Without the gate, any caller could read any user's email тАФ a PII leak that re-opens what the May 25 `profiles_guard_privileged` work closed. For **server-side retention campaigns**: call from an Edge Function with the service role directly off `auth.users`, NOT through this RPC.

**`last_seen_at` тАФ bounded update (avoid token-refresh write amplification):** Supabase already tracks `auth.users.last_sign_in_at`; the reason we duplicate to `profiles.last_seen_at` is RLS-queryability for dormancy cohorts (`auth.users` isn't directly queryable from the client). Update from `ensureProfileForUser()` (`src/lib/auth.js`) + `onAuthStateChange` (`src/lib/authContext.js`), but **gate the write** so token refreshes (тЙИhourly) don't slam the table:
```sql
UPDATE profiles
SET last_seen_at = now()
WHERE id = auth.uid()
  AND (last_seen_at IS NULL OR last_seen_at < now() - interval '5 minutes');
```
For pure dormancy analytics, the existing `events` table + `analytics_dau` view may already suffice тАФ verify before relying on this column.

**Signup streamline тАФ Step 1 of 1 at the auth gate (4 fields):**
- Email ┬╖ password ┬╖ **handle** ┬╖ **`date_of_birth` (full date picker)**
- **Age gate (hard block):** if `now()::date - date_of_birth < interval '13 years'` тЖТ reject with *"You must be 13 or older to create a Rinkd account."* Account is NOT created. (Under-13 minor `profiles` rows happen later via REG-2's household-claim flow тАФ not via self-signup.)
- **Turnstile** renders here (was on the old step 3; widget already wired тАФ just move its mount point).
- **Marketing opt-in checkbox** тАФ defaults UNCHECKED. Label: *"Send me Rinkd news + product updates (you can change this anytime in Settings)."* Sets `notification_email_marketing`. Transactional emails always send.
- On success: create `auth.users`, `ensureProfileForUser()` writes the `profiles` row stamping `date_of_birth` + `notification_email_marketing`; session starts immediately.

**Progressive profile setup тАФ Step 2 (soft prompt, NO wall):**
- First-time users land directly on `/feed` per REG-2 ┬з3.
- **Nudge surfaces:** the existing **`OnboardingModal`** (one-time on first feed view, dismissible) + a dismissible-but-persistent banner atop `/feed` while `profile_complete = false`. **Reuse the existing component patterns** тАФ don't invent new ones.
- **Reward:** +50 points via `add_points()` RPC on completion (genuine optional тЖТ reward is fine, not a dark pattern).
- **Fields:**
  - Full name (existing column)
  - **Persona** (Player / Parent / Coach / Commissioner / Official / Fan) тЖТ `profiles.persona`
  - **Position** (Forward / Defense / Goalie) тЖТ existing `profiles.position`; **only shown when persona = 'player'**
  - Level (Youth тЖТ Beer League тЖТ Fan) тАФ existing column
  - Home rink (optional) тЖТ `profiles.home_rink_id`
  - Gender (optional, inclusive enum тАФ self-reported, never infer or pre-populate) тЖТ `profiles.gender`
  - Avatar тАФ optional, reuse the existing avatar-upload path
- **Live preview** ("Build your player card" / "Set up your locker room") тАФ keep this framing.
- **Completion:** when persona + (position if player) + level are set тЖТ flip `profile_complete = true` тЖТ nudge stops.

**13тАУ17 (minor flag at query time):** `is_minor = (date_of_birth > now()::date - interval '18 years')`. No extra column needed.

**Files to touch:**
- `src/pages/Auth.js` тАФ strip the 3-step wizard to a single step (email / password / handle / DOB picker / marketing checkbox / Turnstile). Drop name/position/level from signup.
- `src/components/OnboardingModal.js` тАФ extend with the progressive fields; gate render on `profile_complete = false`.
- `src/pages/Feed.js` тАФ add the dismissible top banner while `profile_complete = false`.
- `src/lib/auth.js` тАФ `ensureProfileForUser()` accepts `date_of_birth` + `notification_email_marketing`.
- `src/lib/authContext.js` тАФ wire the **bounded** `last_seen_at` update on `onAuthStateChange`.
- `src/pages/Settings.js` тАФ surface the notification toggles (transactional + marketing + push) for self-service later.

**Segmentation unlocked (post-data-collection):**
- Persona тАФ player vs parent vs coach vs commissioner vs official vs fan (entirely different messaging).
- Age cohort тАФ youth (U18) / young adult (18тАУ30) / adult rec (30+).
- Gender тАФ women's-hockey growth audience.
- Engagement tier тАФ existing `profiles.tier` (Mite тЖТ Pro).
- Dormancy тАФ `last_seen_at < now() - interval '14 days'` тЖТ re-engagement cohort.
- Marketing-permission universe тАФ `notification_email_marketing = true` is the legal set for promo sends.

**Status (May 28, 2026):** тЬЕ **Both shipped + live on main** (merge commit `fbe96c2b`, single feature commit `a886f04b`). Migration `user_profile_enrichment` already live on prod (additive only; advisor 0-ERROR). Deviations from the original spec applied as documented at commit time: skipped `home_rink_id` FK (existing TEXT `home_rink` + `rinks` is event-scoped, not a global registry) and skipped `get_user_email()` RPC (`profiles.email` already exists). Both are recoverable if needs change later.

**What's now on main (vs. main before the merge):**
- **Signup:** 3-step wizard тЖТ **1 step** (email ┬╖ password ┬╖ DOB ┬╖ Turnstile ┬╖ marketing-opt-in default UNCHECKED). Handle auto-generated as `user-<UUID-prefix>`. Full name / persona / position / level / gender all collected progressively.
- **OnboardingModal:** role chooser now writes `profiles.persona` (NOT `position`); 6 personas (`commissioner` and `official` added). Flips `profile_complete = true` if a persona is picked.
- **Feed:** new dismissible `ProfileNudgeBanner` тАФ 6 one-tap chips for users who skipped the modal (`welcome_seen=true, profile_complete=false`). Pick тЖТ writes persona + `profile_complete=true` + `add_points(50)`.
- **App.js:** bounded `touchLastSeen()` (тЙе5 min PostgREST gate) wired into both auth-resolve paths.
- **Settings.js:** three live notification toggles wired to `notification_email_transactional` / `_marketing` / `notification_push` (transactional opt-out shows an amber warning).
- **DB:** `date_of_birth date`, `persona text CHECK`, `gender text CHECK`, `last_seen_at timestamptz`, `notification_email_transactional` (default TRUE), `notification_email_marketing` (default FALSE), `notification_push` (default TRUE), `profile_complete` (default FALSE). `guard_profile_privileged_columns()` extended to silently freeze `date_of_birth` after first set for non-admins.

**Original sequencing thesis still holds:** both are **orthogonal to REG-2 Phase 1** (identity spine + `auth_user_id` decouple): REG-2 Phase 1 expects these adult-self-signup columns to already exist and will only add `auth_user_id` / `account_type` / households / consent. `MONEY-1` (Crease subscription) is fully independent and can ship any time.

### `SOCIAL-1` тАФ GameSheet sidecar import + tournament "social-only" mode (spec'd May 28, 2026)

**SKU name (public-facing):** **Rinkd Social.**

**Why:** Nickel City call May 28 validated the additive-wedge play (`docs/OUTREACH_PIPELINE.md` Nickel City row, memory `outreach_playbook`). Matt's words: *"my process isn't broken тАФ can I try it as just the community/engagement piece without disrupting what I already have?"* This SKU answers that тАФ Rinkd runs the social layer on top of an operator's existing scoring (GameSheet / HockeyShift / Spordle) + registration (Regystra / LeagueApps / EventConnect) stack. Zero replacement, additive only. **Lesson reinforced by Matt + memory `outreach_playbook`:** for high-volume nimble operators on rented stacks, the wedge IS the deal тАФ don't pitch replacement.

**Build (~3тАУ5 days):**
1. **GameSheet CSV import (admin uploader).** Two file types Matt exports from GameSheet today:
   - **Teams export** тЖТ upserts into `tournament_teams` (team_name, division if present, contact_email). Nameplate-only, no claim required.
   - **Games export** тЖТ upserts into `tournament_games` (home/away team, time, sheet, period scores, final, optional `external_id` for idempotency).
   - **Idempotent re-import** keyed on `(tournament_id, external_id)` for games + `(tournament_id, team_name)` for teams. Re-running on an updated export silently merges scores. Dry-run preview + commit button in the importer UI.
   - **Where:** `TournamentManage` тЖТ new **Import tab** (director-gated; only visible when `scoring_source = 'external'`).
   - **Migration:** `tournament_games_external_id` тАФ add nullable `external_id text` + unique partial index on `(tournament_id, external_id) where external_id is not null`.
2. **Tournament `scoring_source` mode:**
   ```sql
   ALTER TABLE tournaments
     ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS scoring_source text
       CHECK (scoring_source IN ('rinkd','external')) DEFAULT 'rinkd';
   ```
   When `external`:
   - `ScorerView` is hidden (`canScore` returns false regardless of director status).
   - The Registrations tab is hidden (operator's reg lives elsewhere).
   - Public landing + signed-in tabbed view get a subtle byline: *"Scores & schedule via GameSheet ┬╖ Powered by Rinkd Social."*
   - `submit-scoresheet` Edge Function 409s for any `external`-mode tournament (defensive тАФ UI gates this, the API gates it too).
3. **Auto-recap from import (not from finalize).** In `rinkd`-mode the auto-recap fires on ScorerView finalize. In `external` mode there's no finalize event тАФ the importer triggers it. When the importer first sees a game flip to `home_score != null && away_score != null && status = 'final'`, fire `createGameRecapPost` (existing fn). Idempotent on `(tournament_id, game_id)`.
4. **What still works in `external` mode (unchanged):** Feed tab + chirps composer + photos ┬╖ standings + Stats tab (jersey-keyed тАФ works off imported scores) ┬╖ `send-recap-push` pipeline + tournament Follow + per-game stream URL. This is the moat тАФ most of what makes Rinkd valuable runs read-only off whatever scoring system the operator uses.
5. **Symmetric for leagues (smaller v1):** add `leagues.scoring_source` with the same enum. The full league sidecar is out-of-scope for v1 (Matt is tournaments-only); ship the column + mode-gating now so a league sale isn't blocked later.

**Pricing тАФ Model D (Pete pick May 28, 2026):**

| Tier | Trigger | Price |
|---|---|---|
| **Free** | Tournament with **< 8 teams** | $0 тАФ grassroots loss-leader |
| **Per-event ┬╖ Small** | 8тАУ24 teams | **$99 / event** |
| **Per-event ┬╖ Mid** | 25тАУ74 teams | **$249 / event** |
| **Per-event ┬╖ Large** | 75+ teams | **$499 / event** |
| **Annual (operator)** | Customer picks at activation | **$1,500 / year** тАФ unlimited tournaments + leagues + off-season feed |

**Self-selecting math** is the model's whole trick: high-volume operators (Matt at 24 events/season) self-select into Annual (~$62/event effective vs ~$249 per-event); low-volume operators (1тАУ2 events/year) self-select into per-event. Free <8 teams keeps small organizers on-platform тАФ they build community, graduate paid as they grow.

**Symmetric across leagues:** the **Annual SKU covers leagues + tournaments together** тАФ one operator subscription, all their events. Stand-alone league social-only pricing (for operators not picking Annual) deferred; mirrors the per-event ladder per-season when needed. For v1: any non-Annual league = per-season tier (TBD); any non-Annual tournament = per-event tier (above).

**Pricing-tier column** (added with this build):
```sql
ALTER TABLE tournaments
  ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS pricing_tier text
    CHECK (pricing_tier IN ('free','per_event','annual')) DEFAULT 'free';
ALTER TABLE leagues
  ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS pricing_tier text
    CHECK (pricing_tier IN ('free','per_event','annual')) DEFAULT 'free';
```
Stamped at activation time. Drives the activation gate logic (admin RPC).

**Sales pitch (locked):**
- Lead: тнР *"52-week engagement vs one-weekend transactions."*
- Frame: additive on top of GameSheet / HockeyShift / Spordle + Regystra / LeagueApps / EventConnect тАФ *keep what works.*
- Offer: **free first event** for new customers (pilot foothold), then pick per-event or Annual.

**Customers in play right now:**
- **Nickel City Hockey / Matt Peters** тАФ ЁЯЯв WARM PILOT OPENING (`docs/OUTREACH_PIPELINE.md`). Picks Annual when the time comes (24 events ├Ч $249 = $5,976 vs $1,500 тАФ obvious).
- **Premier Ice Prospects / Kathy Pippy** тАФ same incumbent stack (GameSheet + Regystra), same wedge. Not contacted yet (phase-1).
- **Vaughan Rangers / Silver Stick GTA** тАФ GameSheet + Spordle. Email out May 25, awaiting reply.
- **Anyone on Sportsheadz / SportsEngine / EventConnect / HockeyShift** тАФ different incumbent stack, same additive play; same SKU.

**Pricing-guide source-of-truth:** `docs/Rinkd_Pricing_Guide.docx` тАФ needs a new "Rinkd Social" section added (per memory `pricing_model`'s "canonical in docx" rule). Pete to update or call the docx skill.

**Priority + sequencing:** **P1** (revenue-attached, named warm prospect, ~3тАУ5 days). **No pilot dependency.** Order: ENRICH-1 + ONBOARD-1 (DONE) тЖТ `SOCIAL-1` тЖТ REG-2 Phase 1. `MONEY-1` (Crease subscription) is fully independent and can ship in any slot.

**Deferred / explicit non-goals for v1:**
- HockeyShift / Spordle / other-tool importers тАФ start with GameSheet (highest-leverage named customer). Other importers ship the same migration pattern when a customer names the need.
- Live GameSheet API integration тАФ manual CSV import is fine for v1; auto-sync later if GameSheet exposes an API. (They don't today.)
- Stripe Connect for the Annual SKU тАФ Annual is a recurring subscription, lands on `MONEY-1`'s subscription plumbing when that ships. Per-event uses the existing one-time charge model (polymorphic `stripe-checkout` + `stripe-webhook`, add a `kind: 'tournament_social'`).
- League-side stand-alone social-only ladder pricing тАФ deferred until a league customer asks for it without the Annual SKU.

### ЁЯЪз `MULTIDIV-1` + `SOCIAL-2` тАФ IN PROGRESS on branch `feature/multi-division` (started May 28, 2026) тАФ READ THIS BEFORE CONTINUING

**Decision (Pete, May 28):** build multi-division tournaments NOW (recurring blocker across prospects, not just Nickel City) + build the automated GameSheet results poller (`SOCIAL-2`). Spec for multi-division: `rinkd_v4/MULTI_DIVISION_AND_ELIGIBILITY_BUILD.md` (Phases 1тАУ4). This session built **Phase 1, milestones M1тАУM3.**

**тЪая╕П Pilot guardrail (non-negotiable):** BLPA Cleveland is **Jun 13тАУ14**. Do **NOT** merge `feature/multi-division` to main or touch the live `tournament_standings` view before Jun 14. The schema is additive + the standings rebuild is staged under a temp name precisely so prod stays pilot-safe.

**What's already LIVE ON PROD** (DB migrations applied via Supabase MCP тАФ schema is present regardless of git branch):
- `multidiv_phase1_additive_schema` (M1): new `tournament_divisions` table (RLS: public read + `is_tournament_director` writes); nullable `division_id` on `tournament_teams` (FK ON DELETE CASCADE) + `games` (FK ON DELETE SET NULL); backfill = one **"Main"** division per existing event, every team/game pointed at it. **0 unassigned, advisor 0-ERROR, BLPA byte-identical.**
- `multidiv_phase1_staged_standings_view` (M2): **`tournament_standings_md`** тАФ the division-scoped standings view (rank partitioned by `(tournament_id, division_id, pool)`, per-division `settings` override falling back to tournament settings). **The live `tournament_standings` is UNTOUCHED.** Proven byte-identical to the live view across all events (EXCEPT both ways = 0).
- `multidiv_stats_rpcs_add_optional_division_filter` (Stats follow-up): `get_tournament_skater_stats` + `get_tournament_goalie_stats` gained an optional `p_division_id uuid default null` filtering the single games CTE each funnels through. **NULL = event-wide (today's exact behavior), so this is backward-compatible тАФ `main`/BLPA passes no division arg and is unchanged.** SECURITY INVOKER preserved, advisor 0-ERROR. No M7 cutover needed for stats (the default arg means both `main` and the branch resolve to the same function).

**What's on the BRANCH** (`feature/multi-division`, commit `27f0cf0b`, pushed; Vercel preview alias `rinkd-git-feature-multi-division-...vercel.app`):
- **M3** тАФ `src/pages/Tournament.js`: division switcher chips (only render when >1 division), standings read from the **staged** view via a `const STANDINGS_VIEW = 'tournament_standings_md'` at the top of the file, all divisions loaded once + filtered client-side, Standings/Schedule/Bracket/champion/tiebreakers/advancement scoped to the selected division via a `divSettings` merge. **Single-division events (BLPA) render byte-identical тАФ no switcher.** Stats tab left event-wide (division-scoping the 4 stat RPCs is a follow-up). Build clean.

  - New `src/lib/tournamentDivisions.js`: `listDivisions` / `createDivision` / `updateDivision` / `deleteDivision` / `reorderDivisions`. Reads public; writes via `is_tournament_director` RLS on `tournament_divisions`.

A **scope selector** (chips) renders above Teams/Schedule/Bracket when >1 division and filters those panels to `selectedDivisionId` (same preserve-across-reload pattern as M3). `divSettings` = division.settings over tournament.settings.
  - `src/lib/tournamentManage.js`: same `const STANDINGS_VIEW = 'tournament_standings_md'`; `division_id` threaded through `createTeam`, `generatePoolSchedule` (scopes the round-robin + the replace-existing delete to one division), `createBracketGame`, `generateChampionshipBracket` (scopes seeds + the already-has-bracket guard + tags rows), `loadPoolQualifiers`. `listStandingsSummary` now reads the staged view + carries `division_id`.
  - `src/pages/ScorerView.js`: `resolveBracketSlotsFromSemis(tournamentId, pool, game.division_id)` тАФ now division-scoped so two divisions sharing a pool name ("Pool A") can't cross-wire gold/bronze resolution.
  - **No DDL** (live `tournament_standings` untouched). Build +2.6 kB, advisor 0-ERROR. Verified via a throwaway 2-division sandbox (both pool "A"): the staged view produced two separate, correctly-ranked standings; per-division advancement honored. Closes the gap where *newly-created* events had zero divisions (M1 only backfilled existing ones), so the M4 Divisions tab/scoping now works on new events too. CASCADE-cleaned with the tournament on failure. **No new wizard UI** тАФ single-division flow looks identical; multi-division authoring lives in the Manage тЖТ Divisions tab (Pete's call, May 28). `generateChampionshipBracket` was already division-scoped (M4). Verified the full insert chain (tournament тЖТ division тЖТ teams/games tagged) via a throwaway event, then deleted. Build clean.

Advisor 0-ERROR. Sandbox deleted. **Known follow-up:** the Stats tab is still event-wide (the 4 stat RPCs aren't division-scoped yet) тАФ not a Phase-1 blocker.

**тнР The M7 cutover gotcha:** the branch reads `tournament_standings_md` in **two files now** (`Tournament.js` + `lib/tournamentManage.js`). **At M7 (post-Jun-14):** (1) `DROP VIEW tournament_standings; ALTER VIEW tournament_standings_md RENAME TO tournament_standings;` (2) flip the `STANDINGS_VIEW` constant **in both files** back to `'tournament_standings'`; (3) merge the branch to main. (lib/tournamentManage.js's 3 standings queries are already re-pointed via the constant тАФ just flip it.)

**Remaining milestones:**
- **M7** (тП╕я╕П POST-Jun-14 тАФ do NOT start before the BLPA pilot) тАФ view cutover + merge to main (see the cutover gotcha above). **Phase 1 (M1тАУM6) complete + verified on the branch.**
- **Phases 2тАУ4 тЬЕ DONE on `feature/multi-division`** (May 29):
  - **Phase 4 тАФ rule partials** (commit `99899d12`): `games.forfeit` flag + `recordForfeit()` (3-0 to the winner, no goal log; standings count it off the score, view unchanged) + a Forfeit action on the manage game-edit row. Configurable goal-quotient **display** (`divSettings.gq_formula`: `gf_over_ga` default | `gf_over_gf_plus_ga` with GF+GA=0тЖТ1.0 guard) тАФ display-only, the view's GF/GA still drives the tiebreaker sort. Advisory **mercy/running-time banner** in ScorerView at the format's `max_goal_differential` in P3 (no app clock тАФ GS-3 stays held).
  - **Phase 2 тАФ eligibility (advisory)** (commit `eb370a69`): `tournament_divisions.roster_frozen_at` + `game_lineups.usa_hockey_number` (additive). New `src/lib/eligibility.js` computes flags from jersey-keyed lineups: no-prelim-game, added-after-freeze, missing-USAH# (only once any USAH# is entered). New division-scoped **Eligibility tab** (Freeze/Unfreeze + flag list). Never blocks.
  - **Phase 3 тАФ suspensions (advisory)** (commit `20ee70a9`): `game_suspensions` table (jersey-keyed, division-scoped, director-manages + scorer-can-insert RLS). New `src/lib/suspensions.js`. ScorerView: a Game Misconduct / Match Penalty prompts "Create a suspension?" тЖТ row (`games_remaining=1`). New division-scoped **Suspensions tab** (active vs served, mark-served, manual add, remove). Subsumes GS-2. Advisory.
  - All additive, pilot-safe (inert for BLPA), advisor 0-ERROR, builds clean. **The full `MULTI_DIVISION_AND_ELIGIBILITY_BUILD.md` spec (Phases 1тАУ4) is now built on the branch тАФ only M7 (cutover + merge) remains, post-pilot.**
- **Stats tab division-scoping тАФ тЬЕ DONE** (commit `27f0cf0b`). The tournament skater + goalie stat RPCs took an optional `p_division_id` (live on prod, backward-compatible тАФ see the LIVE ON PROD list above); `StatLeaderboards` threads a `divisionId` prop and `Tournament.js`'s Stats tab passes `selectedDivisionId`, so the leaderboards follow the division switcher. Verified on a 2-division sandbox (event-wide = AтИкB, each division isolated for skaters + goalies). The league stat boards are unaffected (leagues have no divisions).

**`SOCIAL-2` (GameSheet results poller) тАФ S1 + S2 тЬЕ DONE (May 29); S3 (admin UI) next.** Branch `feature/gamesheet-poller` @ `5f6b79d6`. Full API recon + S2/S3 spec: [`rinkd_v4/SOCIAL2_GAMESHEET_API_RECON.md`](../rinkd_v4/SOCIAL2_GAMESHEET_API_RECON.md).
- **S1-finish:** GameSheet's public stats API is fully mapped. Host `gamesheetstats.com`; the poller's one endpoint is **`GET /api/useScoredGames/getSeasonScores/{seasonId}`** тАФ **public, no auth** (Firebase/Cloud-Run auth is only for their admin write features). Returns only *scored* games, each with a stable `gameId`, team names + division, and `finalScore:{homeGoals,visitorGoals}`. (Supporting: `getSeason/{id}`, `getDivisions/{id}`.) Clean JSON pull, not a scrape тАФ but **undocumented/ToS-gray**, treat fail-soft.
- **Model (Pete, May 28):** explicit tables ┬╖ **auto-write on stable-id, confirm-once on first fuzzy match** (never auto-write a fuzzy match тАФ guards against scoring the wrong game) ┬╖ `scoring_source='external'` alongside.
- **S2 built + deployed + verified:** migration `social2_gamesheet_poller_schema` (prod, additive/pilot-safe тАФ `tournaments.scoring_source` 'rinkd'|'external', `gamesheet_links`, `gamesheet_game_map`, director-gated RLS, advisor 0-ERROR) + Edge Function **`sync-gamesheet`** (v1, `verify_jwt=false` + `CRON_KEY` gate). Confirmed maps auto-write the score; first flip-to-final posts a recap (author = director) + fires `send-recap-push`; unseen games fuzzy-match (team names + date) тЖТ PENDING for admin confirm. **Only acts on activated tournaments** (moat-consistent; inert for BLPA). E2E-verified vs real season 6416 (fuzzyтЖТpendingтЖТconfirmтЖТscore+Playoff-recapтЖТidempotent no-op); sandbox deleted.
- тЪая╕П **GO-LIVE OPS (Pete тАФ before linking a real event):** (1) set the **`CRON_KEY`** Supabase secret тАФ the function is currently publicly invokable (CRON_KEY unset + verify_jwt=false); bounded blast radius (can only mirror a partner's *public* scores onto a *linked + activated* event, of which there are none yet), but set it before real use; (2) schedule **pg_cron** `*/3 * * * *` per the header comment in `sync-gamesheet/index.ts`. Same gated-secret pattern as the Stripe webhook secrets.
- **S3 тЬЕ DONE (commit `3b7e66d8`):** director-facing **GameSheet tab** in `TournamentManage` (new `src/lib/gamesheet.js`). Link a season (event-wide v1) тЖТ flips the event to `scoring_source='external'`; shows last-sync status; a **"Needs review"** list confirms/ignores the matches the poller queues (with a manual game-picker for unmatched rows); a **"Synced"** list shows mirrored games. `ScorerView` now shows a read-only "Scores synced from GameSheet" wall when `scoring_source='external'` (the external mode Pete signed off тАФ no dual scoring path). Build clean; director-RLS verified (impersonation, rolled back). **SOCIAL-2 is feature-complete** (S1+S2+S3) on `feature/gamesheet-poller`.
- **External-scoring gate тЬЕ COMPLETE** (commit `62af9e20`): beyond the ScorerView wall, `scoring_source='external'` now also **hides the Registrations tab** in TournamentManage and **`submit-scoresheet` (v13) rejects external tournaments server-side (409)** тАФ defense-in-depth so a manual scoresheet can't bypass the synced scores. This is the SOCIAL-1 external mode Pete signed off, now fully wired.
- **Auto-import (#1) тЬЕ DONE** (commit `1cebdaa8`): the poller creates Rinkd teams + game rows (final + score + recap) for GameSheet games with no existing Rinkd match тАФ so an operator links a season and the schedule + scores materialize, no hand-rebuild. Gated by `gamesheet_links.auto_import` (default on; off = fuzzy-match + confirm onto a pre-built schedule). E2E-verified from an EMPTY event on real BLPA season 14586.
- **Stats embed + recap enrichment (#2) тЬЕ DONE** (commit `66d4778a`): the **Stats gap is solved by display, not ingestion** тАФ for external events the public Stats tab embeds GameSheet's own recolored `/players`+`/goalies` widget (confirmed `frame-ancestors *`, no X-Frame-Options; Skaters/Goalies toggle; branding stripped via `configuration[...]` params; "Open on GameSheet" fallback). `createLink` stashes `gamesheet_season_id` in public `tournaments.settings` so the public page can build the iframe URL. Native Rinkd-scored events keep the jersey-keyed RPC boards. **Recaps now list goal scorers** from the GameSheet `recap[]` ("Goals: Name ├ЧN"). тЪая╕П Stats are **GameSheet-owned (displayed via iframe), not data we own** тАФ fine for the additive play; *owned* stat data + player profiles need ingestion + identity-mapping (separate later track тАФ see below). Recommend a live branch-preview eyeball of the embedded tab.
- **Still open on SOCIAL-2:** (a) **GO-LIVE OPS** тАФ set `CRON_KEY` + schedule pg_cron (above); until then the poller only runs on manual invoke. (b) **Per-division linking** тАФ schema + poller support it; the link form is event-wide until the multi-division UI merges (M7). (c) **SOCIAL-1 CSV import** тАФ BLOCKED on a real GameSheet CSV sample (likely moot for GameSheet operators тАФ the poller covers them). (d) **Owned stat data + player profiles** (future track): the iframe is display-only; to own stats (cross-event, career, profiles) we'd ingest GameSheet's per-player JSON (findable, same as the scores endpoint) **and** solve GameSheet-player тЖТ Rinkd-user identity mapping (the hard part тАФ needs a claim flow, not fuzzy name-matching). (e) Branch is off `main`, mergeable independently of multi-division (additive/pilot-safe).

- **`SOCIAL-3` тАФ Post-game MVP poll (backlog, social feature idea):** attach a "vote for game MVP / hard-hat" **poll** to the auto-generated game-recap post тАФ a strong post-game re-engagement hook ("get in the car тЖТ vote MVP тЖТ drop photos/chirps"). **New capability:** Rinkd posts don't support polls today (only likes/comments), so this needs a poll primitive on `posts` (options + per-user votes + results render) тАФ reusable beyond recaps. Surfaced by a May 29 Gemini ideation pass; works for both Rinkd-scored and GameSheet-fed events (it hangs off the recap post, which both produce). Not pilot-blocking; P2-ish engagement play.

**Pricing note:** `SOCIAL-1` Model D pricing is the **public** SKU. Nickel City is a one-off **Founding Partner** deal (year-one $0 тЖФ co-marketing) тАФ see `docs/Rinkd_x_NickelCity_Partnership_Proposal.{md,pdf}`. Don't conflate the two: other GameSheet operators get Model D; Nickel City is the named exception.

### `GROUPS-1` тАФ Community groups (open social pages, no team/league required) тАФ SPEC'd Jun 1, 2026

**Why:** Today every Rinkd feed is anchored to a competition object тАФ global, a `tournament`, or a `league` (see memories `tournament_scoped_feed`, `league_scoped_feed_and_push`). There's no home for the *unstructured* hockey community: a metro-area beer-league crowd, a pickup/drop-in crew, a rink's regulars, a "who's got a sub Thursday at 10:40?" group. **Groups** are user-created community pages тАФ e.g. *"Metro Detroit Beer League"* тАФ where people **talk, post, and ask for fill-ins/subs without standing up a team or a league.** Strategic value: (1) lowest-possible-barrier acquisition тАФ anyone spins one up in 20 seconds, no roster/schedule/activation; (2) captures the enormous slice of beer-league hockey that will never be a *managed* Rinkd league but is exactly our user; (3) the **sub/fill-in request** is a genuine high-frequency pain point тЖТ recurring, real-utility engagement (not just chirps), which pulls people back daily. It's a network-effect/retention play, free by design.

**Hard line vs. teams/leagues/tournaments (this is what keeps it simple):** a Group has **NO scoring, NO standings, NO stats, NO bracket, NO activation gate.** It is a *social-only* primitive тАФ feed + members + sub board. If a group ever wants schedules/standings, that's the cue to spin up a real league (upsell path). Resisting scope-creep here is the whole design.

**Reuse (most of this already exists тАФ Groups is largely a 4th scope on the feed):**
- **Feed/composer/comments/reactions/photos** тАФ add `posts.group_id` exactly like `tournament_id` / `league_id` (NULL = not a group post; global/following queries already filter the scope cols to NULL). The entire composer + scoped-feed + `is_hidden` moderation filter (memory `image_moderation_gate_off`) works unchanged.
- **Push** тАФ reuse the `notifications` тЖТ AFTER-INSERT trigger тЖТ pg_net тЖТ `send-notification-push` pipeline (memory `social_push_and_live_strip`). New `kind`s: `group_sub` (a sub request posted to a group you're in), `group_join` (request to join, to owner/admin).
- **Join-request flow** тАФ mirror the team manager/join pattern (`team_members` + request тЖТ approve; memory `team_roster_management`).
- **Sub respondents** тАФ "I'll cover it" routes to a **DM** via `getOrCreateDm` (memory `direct_messages`), or a comment thread on the request.
- **Blocks** тАФ respect `user_blocks` everywhere (no notify, hide posts both directions).

**Model (additive; SECURITY-INVOKER views per memory `security_definer_views`):**
- `groups` тАФ `id, slug (unique), name, description, location_text (e.g. "Metro Detroit, MI"), avatar_url, banner_url, visibility ('public'|'private'|'unlisted') default 'public', created_by тЖТ profiles, created_at`. (Geo lat/lng deferred тАФ `location_text` is enough for v1 search.)
- `group_members` тАФ `group_id тЖТ groups, user_id тЖТ profiles, role ('owner'|'admin'|'member'), status ('active'|'pending'|'banned'), joined_at`. Creator inserted as `owner` on create (mirrors `createTeam`'s founder row). **`is_group_admin(group_id)`** helper (owner immutable), same shape as `is_team_manager` / `is_league_commissioner`.
- `posts.group_id uuid null тЖТ groups` (FK SET NULL) + partial index `(group_id, created_at desc) where group_id is not null`.
- `group_sub_requests` тАФ `id, group_id, author_id тЖТ profiles, play_date timestamptz, location_text, position ('any'|'forward'|'defense'|'goalie'), skill_level text null, notes text, status ('open'|'filled'|'cancelled') default 'open', filled_by тЖТ profiles null, created_at`. Posting a sub request **auto-creates a group feed post** (reuse the recap-post pipeline) so it shows in-feed AND on a structured "Subs" board; flipping to `filled` updates both. **Goalie-needed is the killer case** тАФ surface it.
- **RLS:** public/unlisted groups тЖТ world-readable; private тЖТ active members only. Posting/sub-requesting тЖТ active member (insert-own). Moderation (delete post, ban member, approve join) тЖТ `is_group_admin`. Membership self-insert: public = direct `active`; private = `pending` until an admin flips it.

**Surfaces / IA (phone-first, progressive disclosure per memory `unified_platform_design_mandate`):**
- `/groups` тАФ **directory**: search + filter by `location_text`, "Groups near you" / "Popular", a prominent **Create group** button. Lives in the **desktop sidebar + Discover**; **NOT a new mobile bottom-nav slot** (the bottom bar is intentionally capped at 4 тАФ memory's June 1 nav-polish entry), so reach it from Discover/profile.
- `/groups/:slug` тАФ group page: **Feed** (default) ┬╖ **Subs** (open requests, "Post a sub request" CTA) ┬╖ **Members** ┬╖ **About**. Join/Leave button top-right; private groups show "Request to join". Owner/admin see a lightweight Manage affordance (edit, approve requests, remove posts, ban).
- **Create flow** тАФ one screen: name тЖТ location тЖТ short description тЖТ visibility. That's it. No roster, no schedule, no payment. Dead-simple is the point.

**Effort & phasing (~4тАУ6 days for P1+P2 thanks to feed reuse):**
- **Phase 1 тАФ the place to talk (~2тАУ3 d):** `groups` + `group_members` + `posts.group_id` + `is_group_admin` + create flow + `/groups` directory + `/groups/:slug` (Feed/Members/About) + public-join / private-request. Ships the core "community without a team/league."
- **Phase 2 тАФ the differentiated hook (~1.5тАУ2 d):** `group_sub_requests` + Subs board + auto-post to group feed + `group_sub` push to members + "I'll cover it" тЖТ DM. This is the daily-active driver тАФ don't skip it, it's the reason a group beats a Facebook group.
- **Phase 3 (later):** geo discovery (lat/lng + distance sort), group categories, richer moderation, per-member notification granularity (a `group_subscriptions` opt-in like `league_subscriptions` if "notify me about this group" needs to be separate from membership).

**Guardrails:** respect `user_blocks` end-to-end; suppress self-notify; cap sub-request spam (rate-limit per author/day); `is_hidden`/report infra applies to group posts; private-group content must never leak into global/following/Discover. Owner can't be removed/demoted (immutable, like founder).

**Monetization:** **free** тАФ this is an acquisition/retention/network-effect lever, not a SKU. (Possible *later*: a "verified/pro group" tier or sponsored-group placement, and groups feed the `SOCIAL` top-of-funnel by getting unaffiliated players onto the platform before any league/tournament relationship exists.)

**Open design Qs for Pete (sign off before building, per `unified_platform_design_mandate`):** (1) Sub requests as a **structured table** (recommended тАФ date/position/status, filterable, "goalie needed" surfacing) vs. just a post `kind`/tag? (2) **Default visibility** public vs. private? (3) Should groups be **discoverable by location** in v1 (`location_text` search) or just by name/invite-link? (4) Any **abuse ceiling** тАФ max groups created per user, approval before a group is publicly listed? (5) Does a group get a **DM-style group chat** (extends the DM `type='team'` work) or is the feed enough for v1?

---

### `LA-9` / `SUBS-1` / `SUB-ALERT-1` / `GOALIE-1` тАФ Draft leagues & tournaments + ESHL subs pools + goalie-in-net capture тАФ SPEC'd Jun 4, 2026

**Full spec: [`rinkd_v4/DRAFT_LEAGUE_AND_TOURNAMENT_BUILD.md`](../rinkd_v4/DRAFT_LEAGUE_AND_TOURNAMENT_BUILD.md)** (data model, RLS, migrations, phased milestones, guardrails тАФ modelled on the MULTIDIV build doc). **Drivers:** **CAHL** (Cincinnati Adult Hockey League тАФ Tommy Horan; 1,750 players / 75 teams / 14 divisions; hand-builds balanced teams from a skill-sorted free-agent pool every season тАФ the workflow Rinkd must own to win the account) + **BLPA** draft-format tournaments + **ESHL** (Eastside Shaker Hockey League тАФ Josh Heyka; by-player registration + a subs pool). This **defines the `LA-9` parity gap** (note: `LEAGUEAPPS_PARITY_GAPS.md` had no LA-9 entry тАФ this doc + a new Gap-9 stub now define it).

**`LA-9` тАФ the shared primitive (Phase 1, ~1-1.5 wk, league-first):** one polymorphic `draft_registrations` table (account-required self-reg; skill **1-10 + tier** enum + **F/D/G** position; `preferred_division_id`); opt-in `leagues.draft_open` (default OFF тЖТ existing leagues render byte-identical); commissioner **Draft Pool** tab (sort/filter by skill/position/division/date, **server-side** division filter, paginate at CAHL's 1,750); `assign_draft_player` RPC тЖТ **real `team_members`** via `create_league_team` (do NOT reuse `assign_league_team_manager` тАФ it mints managers + grabs the founder seat); `league_draft_balance` view (security_invoker) for the even-teams indicator; in-app `draft_assignment` notification (no push storm). **Conflict-avoidance (all in the spec guardrails):** `team_members.team_id тЖТ teams.id` so assignment needs a *backed* team, not a nameplate `league_team`; a **NEW sibling table** (don't overload the team-shaped `*_registrations`); a NEW Stripe `kind` branched first in BOTH edge fns (Phase 4); `preferred_division_id` `ON DELETE SET NULL`; PostgREST embed-ambiguity (audit `assigned_by` is FK-less); index every FK + `(parent_id, status, created_at)`. **Phases:** 1 league pool тЖТ 2 live snake draft (optional) тЖТ 3 tournament surface (**POST-pilot, after `feature/multi-division` merges** тАФ tournaments have no roster table today) тЖТ 4 paid per-player Stripe reg. **Locked (Pete, Jun 4):** league-first; numeric+tier skill; free pool in Ph1; account-required self-reg.

**ESHL subs extension (spec ┬з9):**
- **`SUBS-1` (~1.5-2 wk atop LA-9):** per-division **subs pools** тАФ **two** non-scheduled `league_team`s per division (`is_sub_pool` + `sub_pool_kind ('skater'|'goalie')`, unique per `(league_id, division_id, sub_pool_kind)`), **excluded from schedule + standings**. Subs are accounts тЖТ stats are **`user_id`/name-keyed** (NOT jersey тАФ their number changes game-to-game) and render on **each pool's own team page** (Skater Subs / Goalie Subs), isolated from the jersey-keyed boards. **Day-of sub insertion** into a playing team's `game_lineups` (plumbing exists тАФ accepts `user_id` without a `team_members` row); **commissioner + team managers** can add. Plus `registration_open_at` (~0.5 d) for the "reg opens August" scheduled-open gap.
- **`SUB-ALERT-1` (~1-2 d):** sub comms reuse the **team feed** (sub pools are `league_team`s тЖТ free team feed; **no chat build** тАФ verified `conversations` is 1:1-only, so group chat / "unlimited DM" was dropped). Only special behavior: a **"Sub Needed" post** (`posts.is_sub_request` boolean) тЖТ AFTER-INSERT trigger fans a **pushed** notification (`kind='sub_needed'` тАФ add to the push trigger WHEN clause + `KIND_TITLE`) to every pool member. Bounded fan-out, batched.

**`GOALIE-1` тАФ goalie-in-net capture (~3-5 d):** league scoring today does **not** capture which goalie was in net, so the league goalie board is per-team (STAT-leaderboards memo). `GOALIE-1` makes the scorer record **the goalie in net** (per goal/period + goalie changes via existing `game_goalie_changes`) and supports **multiple goalies per team roster**. Unblocks **per-goalie league GAA/SV%** (KOHA stats gap #1) **and goalie *sub* stats** (`SUBS-1` ships the goalie pool as roster+comms until this lands).

**Timeline:** `LA-9` Phase 1 (player registration) is the gating deliverable with a hard **August** deadline (ESHL reg opens August). Subs + goalie capture follow. All POST-pilot relative to BLPA Cleveland (Jun 13-14), but **`LA-9` Ph1 before August** for ESHL.

### `COACH-1`тАж`COACH-4` тАФ Coach & Trainer Pages (third surface: microsites + sessions + content + paid registration) тАФ SPEC'd Jun 5, 2026 (v2, coach-centric)

**Full spec: [`rinkd_v4/TRAINER_COACH_PAGES_BUILD.md`](../rinkd_v4/TRAINER_COACH_PAGES_BUILD.md)** (data model, RLS, indexes, phased milestones, guardrails тАФ modelled on the MULTIDIV doc; **evolved in place** from the trainer draft тЖТ coach-centric `coach_*` schema, `/coach/:slug`, `kind='coach_session'`). **Net-new third surface** тАФ **NOT a LeagueApps parity gap**. **Drivers:** (a) skills trainers stuck on Google Forms + Venmo; (b) the **Jun-5 Coaches Site call (Jamie Henry)** тЖТ a coach-development **content partnership** (they have the content, Rinkd has the coaches). `coach_profiles.coach_type` = `'trainer'|'coach'|'both'`. Additive + opt-in; POST-pilot. (IDs renamed from `TRAINER-*`.)

**Locked (Pete, Jun 5):** (1) **Stripe Connect Express per coach** тАФ paid sessions destination-charge minus **5%** (reuse `stripe-connect` + `stripe_connect_accounts` by the coach's `profiles.id`; required to publish a paid session, free skips it; **0 connected accounts today**); (2) **login-less reg + email auto-link on signup**; (3) **real crawler OG/prerender now** (`COACH-OG-1` тАФ edge middleware + dynamic OG + `sitemap.xml`); (4) **full-microsite branding**; (5) **content (Phase 2) is FREE + manual embed links** тАФ partnership ingestion API = reserved open design, NOT built v1 (`source`/`external_id` hooks); (6) **moderation reuses `is_hidden` + `content_reports`** (no new system); (7) recurrence-ready schema, single-date in P1.

**`COACH-1` тАФ Phase 1 core (~2.5тАУ3 wk):** 3 additive tables тАФ `coach_profiles` (slug, `coach_type`, branding jsonb, `specialty_tags`, status, verified/featured, `is_hidden`), `coach_sessions` (date(s), rink/location, price/capacity/waitlist, recurrence-ready, status, `is_hidden`), `coach_registrations` (player-shaped, login-less, idempotency + anti-double-register partial-uniques). RLS via `is_coach_owner` (public read published+visible; owner CRUD; registrant self-read). Add **`kind='coach_session'`** to BOTH Stripe edge fns тАФ **branched first**. Public microsite `/coach/:slug`, public register `/coach/:slug/session/:id/register` (clone of `LeagueRegister`), owner dashboard `/coach/manage`, onboarding wizard `/coach/create`, **basic `/coaches` directory** (server-side filter by type/specialty/location). **`COACH-OG-1`** (prerender/OG) + **moderation** (`is_hidden` on every public coach entity, reads filter it, reports + admin-hide, image-moderation on uploads) ship in Phase 1. **Conflict-avoidance:** Connect-required-for-paid; **paid capacity is soft** (webhook-confirm race тЖТ confirm-time enforce + waitlist/refund overflow; free hard-caps in one RPC); embed-ambiguity on `coach_registrationsтЖТprofiles`; index every FK; `security_invoker` views.

**`COACH-2` тАФ coaching content layer (~4тАУ6 d):** a Content tab on the microsite тАФ new `coach_content` (title, embed `media_url` [YouTube/Vimeo, **not** raw-video hosting], `content_type`, tags, `is_hidden`, `source`/`external_id`). **Free + manual links v1.** The **partnership ingestion API** (Coaches Site syndication via a signed `coach-content-ingest` webhook upserting `source='the_coaches_site'` rows) is **reserved/open-design тЖТ built in `COACH-4`** if the deal firms. Same `is_hidden` moderation.

**`COACH-3` тАФ player-profile Training section (~3тАУ4 d):** "Training" section on `Profile.js` from `coach_registrations` by `player_id` (confirmed) тЖТ sessions+coach; history **alongside stats** (the long-term moat). Auto-link backfills as login-less registrants sign up. `get_player_training_history` RPC. Default public + hide toggle.

**`COACH-4` тАФ recurring + partnership API + extras (~1тАУ1.5 wk):** RRULE recurring sessions; the partnership **content-ingest API**; waitlist auto-promote; refund automation (Stripe + app-fee reversal); verified/featured admin flows; advanced search (`pg_trgm`) + programmatic SEO landing; custom domain.

**Effort:** ~5.5тАУ6.5 wk full; **Phase 1 (~2.5тАУ3 wk) is the sellable MVP** (larger because of full-microsite + real-OG + Connect + moderation); a **~1тАУ1.5 wk "lite" cut** (standard branding, client-side SEO, free-only, no directory) exists in spec ┬з6. **Open questions (spec ┬з8):** verified-badge criteria, minors/waiver, **content-partnership API design (push/pull/embed, opt-in, rev-share)**, coach discovery nav placement, featured = free vs paid SKU, auto-confirm vs approval, training-history visibility, one-profile-per-user, reviews/ratings, content monetization later.
